He hoped that the satisfactory results of the Argentine negotiations could be announced soon, and that the commercial treaties established with Norway and Denmark could also expand trade. Negotiations between Britain and Sweden are currently making good progress, and a commercial treaty with Germany has also been established. As a result, the amount of British coal exported to Germany will be more than doubled. Minister of Health Young announced changes to the government's unemployment relief policy, saying that the government would propose a bill to assist all able-bodied unemployed people, including those who should not receive unemployment benefits, with the government bearing the administrative and financial responsibility. This move would alleviate the burden of poverty relief on local governments. The impeachment motion was subsequently defeated by a vote of 384 to 46.

Another Stunning Development in the Moscow Trial 87

MacDonald Reverses His Testimony and Pleads Not Guilty

Claims Previous Guilty Plea Was Due to Compelling Circumstances

(Reuters, Moscow, 13th) At the resumption of the trial of the six British engineers this morning at ten o'clock, there was a stunning development. The defendant MacDonald, in a loud and determined voice, stated, "I am indeed innocent," completely reversing his previous confession of guilt. He also declared that he had never instructed Gussev's assistant, Sokolov, to engage in sabotage. The prosecutor asked, "Then why did you confess guilt in your previous statements?" He replied, "Because under certain circumstances, I believed it was expedient to admit guilt, so I confessed guilt yesterday." The prosecutor asked again, "Do you admit guilt today?"

He replied, "No. I say I am indeed innocent. I gave Gussev and others 2,500 rubles for their overtime work. Half of this money was paid by the company, and half was paid by me." The prosecutor then presented MacDonald with his own written confession, which contained statements about obtaining secret information from Sokolov, among other things. The prosecutor asked, "If you deny it today, why did you write it yourself at the time?" MacDonald replied, "Under the circumstances at the time, it was more convenient to write this confession." The number of people attending the trial was not as large as yesterday, as today was a regular workday. Upon hearing MacDonald's statement, they were all shocked. At the same time, the sound system suddenly broke down, making it even more difficult for listeners to understand the questions and answers. Furthermore, the meaning of MacDonald's statements was unclear in several places, requiring frequent calls for interpreters to explain. Yesterday, MacDonald appeared haggard and unwell, but today his demeanor was different. Although he limped slightly on his left foot, he stood upright before the court and denied the allegations in the indictment and in his own written confession in a calm and determined manner. At this point, the trial was adjourned for twenty minutes.

Upon resumption of the trial, the prosecutor cross-examined the defendant Thornton. Thornton denied all the charges. The prosecutor asked, "Did you hear the sound of the airplane engine?" Thornton replied, "Yes, the airplane engine did make a loud noise." The prosecutor said, "Why did you make incorrect statements before?" Thornton replied, "Because my nerves were disordered. The seriousness of the charges made me uneasy." The judge asked, "When did your nerves recover?" Thornton replied, "My nerves returned to normal on the evening of April 4th when I was released." Russian officials interrogated MacDonald and Thornton separately, but MacDonald claimed that he was unaware of any espionage activities by Monkhouse and Cushing. Thornton also stated that he was unaware of any sabotage or espionage by MacDonald, and if he had known, he would have fired MacDonald long ago. At this point, MacDonald suddenly shouted, "He knows about this espionage activity. His testimony this morning is full of contradictions, because MacDonald has been imprisoned for a long time and does not know the full situation."

After the second recess, MacDonald's condition changed again. When the prosecutor asked him whether he admitted to espionage, MacDonald admitted it in a low voice, saying that Thornton had initiated it and that other engineers in the company were also involved. He also admitted that he himself had issued orders to destroy machinery. The court then summoned Thornton to the stand. This time, the questioning was conducted by Deputy Prosecutor Roginsky, whose main purpose was to prove that Thornton had obtained secret information provided by Gussev through MacDonald. Thornton replied, "I don't think I ever instructed any engineer to seek secret information. I don't remember ordering Gussev to seek it either." The court then summoned MacDonald to the stand.

MacDonald directly admitted that he had obtained secret information from Gussev and passed it on to Thornton. The court repeatedly summoned MacDonald and Thornton to the stand, questioning them in turn. MacDonald admitted almost everything the prosecutor asked, while Thornton denied everything from beginning to end. Thornton claimed that he never received any military information from MacDonald, and that he only obtained information related to the Vickers Company. He had stated in his previous confession in prison that he and MacDonald had collected secret information, but he now wanted to delete the word "secret." The court then read out his confession, which implied that all the British engineers were involved in espionage. Thornton claimed that although he had written the document, he wanted to delete this section. Thornton said, "When I wrote this document, I didn't know what I was writing. It was a completely

unconscious text. What I saw and heard in a completely different environment frightened me and induced me to write this. I now wish to correct it." The prosecutor re-examined the two defendants about the money matters. Thornton presented written evidence proving that he had personally purchased fake cloth at a low price, and had lent money to MacDonald, as well as MacDonald's repayment of the loan. The prosecutor turned to MacDonald and asked if there were more than just this one instance of handling funds. MacDonald replied that there were more than just this one instance. The prosecutor asked MacDonald, "If one person in the Vickers Company had received funds for illegal activities, then others in the company must have known about it." MacDonald replied, "Yes." When Thornton was questioned about this, he denied that anyone in the company was involved in espionage, saying that the people in the company only collected harmless information. The prosecutor asked about the

definition of "espionage." Thornton replied, "Espionage is the act of seeking official secrets through illegal means." He also said, "What I can say with certainty now is that the confession I signed is not accurate and was written under mental pressure." The prosecutor asked lengthy questions again, asking Thornton whether he intended to carry out sabotage and slowdowns. Thornton replied, "I have always been engaged in construction and have never engaged in destruction." Thornton's answers remained unwavering. MacDonald, on the other hand, was extremely exhausted and could barely answer. When Monkhouse was questioned, he

firmly denied that he was guilty, and only knew that the company, in order to increase its profits, had given Durgoff, the general manager of the electrical appliance import company, 3,000 rubles. Monkhouse also said that the document he signed admitting to bribing Durgoff was not written by him. Gussev and his assistant Sokolov testified that they did not know Monkhouse and had never had any dealings with him. Finally, MacDonald stated that in prison, he had written to the Political Detective Bureau and the court with certain requests, but he did not wish to disclose the contents in court at this time. At this point, the court adjourned. A certain Russian observer whispered to the Reuters reporter, "Do you know that Soviet Russia has spent a total of 25 million rubles on this case? As for the amount of bribery involved in the case, it is only enough to buy a few typewriters." Chen Bozhi, the son of Chinese

Chen Youren, also attended the hearing today.

The U.S. President's Wife Falls While Horseback Riding, Remains Calm 88

(National, Washington, 13th) U.S. President Roosevelt's wife was horseback riding in Potomac Park today when her horse was startled by a car, stumbled backward, and threw Mrs. Roosevelt to the ground. The same is true of the Vickers Electrical Company itself. This company has never had any relationship with the Detective Bureau.

The Four-Power Pact Will Be Established 89

British Public Opinion Does Not Support Helping Germany Revise the Treaty of Versailles

Labour Party Leader Criticizes Simon for Ignoring the Sino-Japanese Dispute

(Reuters, London, 13th) The British House of Commons debated diplomatic matters before adjourning for the Easter recess today. Foreign Secretary Simon spoke of the Four-Power Pact, saying that he would soon be able to place documents related to this matter before the House for discussion.

The rumors circulating about this pact do not apply to the Rome talks. Some say that the British Prime Minister and he were induced to support the Italian plan. This is purely castles in the air. The British Prime Minister and he had only carefully studied the Italian plan. The British government is determined not to collude with any other country and impose its own will on others. Foreign Secretary Simon also spoke of the situation in Germany, saying that Britain now has an important concession, allowing German Jews to go to Palestine. The entire House, in view of the situation in Germany, expressed disapproval of the Four-Power Pact. Member of Parliament Attlee stated that he acknowledged that Germany was demanding fair treatment, but if Germany wanted to revise the treaty, it must show that it treated people fairly. Former Foreign Secretary Chamberlain stated that now is not the time to allow a country that claims that those who advocate peace or are Jewish are guilty to revise the treaty or grant concessions. Mrs. Rathbone, a non-partisan member representing British universities, stated that the malignant revival of Germany is not a blessing for world peace and freedom. Labour Party member Wedgwood stated that Germany itself has destroyed attempts to revise the treaty, but he asked Britain to allow victims in Germany to take refuge in Britain, as it has always done. Churchill stated that if Germany obtains complete military equality, the date for the resumption of the European War will not be far off. Foreign Secretary Simon made a reply to the above opinions, saying that Britain has the same feelings for the treatment of minorities in Germany. British officials in Palestine have issued licenses allowing 1,000 German working-class Jews to move to their Jewish homeland before the end of September. In the future, another 200 entry permits will be issued, allowing German Jews with capital of 1,000 pounds to enter. As for those with skills but without such capital, their entry may also be approved at discretion. At the end of the debate, Labour Party leader Lansbury criticized the Foreign Secretary for not saying a word about the Sino-Japanese dispute, and hoped that the Foreign Secretary would handle the matter as soon as possible. The House then adjourned until April 25.

Conflicts of Interest Between Japan and Russia in the Northeast 97

On the Surface, It Is a Dispute Between the Puppet State and Soviet Russia

In Reality, It Is a Secret Struggle Between Japan and Russia

Even a Temporary Understanding Is Impossible

Harbin Dispatch: Recently, the relationship between the puppet state of Manchuria and Soviet Russia has become increasingly tense. This situation, on the surface, is a conflict between the puppet state and Soviet Russia, but in reality, it is a conflict of interests between Japan and Russia. Therefore, this kind of situation cannot be resolved in fact, and even a temporary understanding is difficult to establish. Aggravating each other, resentment is accumulating, and the points of contention are worth mentioning to the people of the country.

National Border Demarcation Issue 98

After the puppet state was established, it immediately planned to demarcate the national border with Soviet Russia. It is undoubtedly due to the instigation of the Japanese side. However, because military affairs were busy at the time, it was inconvenient to negotiate with the Russian side. After the fall of Rehe, the so-called puppet state territory has been completed. The Japanese side then instructed the puppet state to formally propose the issue of border demarcation to Soviet Russia, requesting the Russian side to send representatives to negotiate with the puppet state representatives. The Soviet Russian authorities originally knew the Japanese intention, and refused to discuss it on the grounds that they had not yet recognized the puppet state. The puppet state then sent Xie Bu-liu-bin from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs as a representative to Harbin to negotiate with the Russian side. According to the Russian newspapers here, Xie's visit was entrusted with the mission of promoting a meeting between Soviet Russia and the puppet state. The content was to be discussed by representatives from the three countries of Soviet Russia, the puppet state, and Japan. The scope of the discussion, in addition to the delineation of the borders between the three countries, also included the navigation rights of the Songhua River and the Kerulen River. The puppet state suggested that the meeting be held in Harbin, but the Russian side had neither clearly expressed this nor made any preparations. It is evident that this matter is still far from resolution, and it is unlikely to be realized in the near future.

Su Bingwen Issue 99

After General Su Bingwen retreated from northern Manchuria into Russian territory, the Japanese side instigated the puppet state to demand his extradition, which was rejected by the Russian side. The Japanese were extremely dissatisfied. Recently, the Soviet Russian authorities allowed General Su and about 1,000 of his subordinates to leave Russia and enter Rehe, which was obviously unfavorable to the puppet state. The Japanese believe that this move by Moscow is entirely an unfriendly attitude and suspect that it has a threatening effect. Therefore, they instigated the puppet state's Ministry of Foreign Affairs to order its representative in Harbin to lodge a serious protest with the Soviet Consul General in Harbin, but the Russian Consul Snovaski did not reply, saying that such a note should be submitted to the Soviet central government, and whether to reply should also be considered by Moscow.

Arrest of Puppet Diplomatic Official 100

Li, a secretary of the puppet state's consulate in Heihe, was arrested and detained for four hours by the local Russian police on March 27. He was released upon the request of Shi Hongchi, the consul of the consulate. The puppets of the puppet state regard this as a great insult and have decided to protest to Moscow. The details of Li's arrest are not yet known. The protest letter is still being studied, and it is difficult to predict how to word it or when to send it.

Chinese Eastern Railway Car Detention Issue 101

Koslersov, the Russian Deputy Director of the Chinese Eastern Railway Bureau, recently ordered the Russian section chief to detain several train heads and many railway materials that had entered Russian territory and not allow them to be returned. This matter is very serious. The puppet state government has sent the Deputy Minister of Transportation and the Chief of the Fifth Section of the Ministry of Transportation (both Japanese) to Harbin to investigate the truth and negotiate with Russia. The Director of the Chinese Eastern Railway Bureau (now appointed by the puppet state) has already submitted a written question to the Russian section chief of the railway on March 18, requesting a clear reply before noon on March 24, but the Russian section chief believes that there is no need to explain this matter and ignored it. The representatives of the Ministry of Transportation of the puppet state are extremely dissatisfied and have decided to stay for a few more days to negotiate directly with the Deputy Director of the railway. According to sources here, the representatives of the puppet state have already met with the Deputy Director, but have not obtained any key information. The Deputy Minister of the puppet state recently told people that he was very angry about the illegal detention of cars by the Russian side, saying that the arbitrary actions of the Russian section chief are absolutely unforgivable. If, in future negotiations, Russia still does not sincerely consider the legitimate demands of the puppet state, he will report all the facts to the puppet state government and await orders. The representative of the puppet state also solemnly declared that the puppet state government has established an overall plan for the development of Manchuria, and no matter what the attitude of the Russian side is, it will never change its policy. This statement is tantamount to demonstrating to the Russian side, but it is expected that the Russian authorities will not be intimidated by the Japanese, and it is feared that the conflict between Russia and Japan will become more apparent as a result. (March 28)

After the Loss of Lengkou, Our Army Increased Support and Counterattacked 102

Our army temporarily retreated to a new position inside the pass.

Shang Zhen ordered that the lost territory be recovered within a time limit.

Luandong has been affected and has become tense.

A special dispatch from Beiping: After the Japanese army's invasion of Luandong failed, it launched a fierce attack on various passes of the Great Wall, and bombarded Fengfengkou and Gubeikou to contain our army's forces. On the other hand, it used its main forces to attack Lengkou fiercely. Our army's front was too long, and it divided its troops to defend against the enemy. The allocation of troops to various small passes was inevitably slightly thin. The Japanese used the puppet army to copy small roads, sneak into the pass, and disturb our rear. Our garrison in Lengkou fought fiercely with the enemy for three days and nights. Several people on the front were defeated, and Japanese puppet troops had rushed into the small passes on both wings. Our army, fearing encirclement, abandoned the Lengkou Changying area positions at 11:30 AM yesterday (11th) and retreated to Tiger Mountain and Guanyintang, etc., waiting for reinforcements to counterattack. Today (12th), some troops have been ordered to rush to the Lengkou area to reinforce the battle and strive to reverse the situation. Shang Zhen has also ordered his troops to restore Lengkou within a time limit. The course of the Lengkou battle is briefly described as follows:

The Japanese troops attacking Lengkou this time were the Hattori and Suzuki brigades and the Cheng Guorui's puppet army, totaling more than 10,000, with more than 30 aircraft, 40 to 50 artillery pieces, and 30 armored vehicles and tanks. The troops stationed in that area were two brigades of Shang Zhen's troops. The rear reserve team originally had some troops. Because of the emergency in Luandong, they were transferred to increase the force, so the force in that area was relatively thin. Starting on the 9th, the Japanese army began to invade, first using more than 30 aircraft and 40 to 50 mountain and field guns to bombard our outer positions fiercely, non-stop all day long. The fortifications of our outer positions were mostly destroyed by bombing. On the 10th, the Japanese puppet infantry and cavalry charged at our positions under the cover of artillery and aircraft. The two sides engaged in melee combat dozens of times. Our army fought bravely and killed many enemies. The enemy failed to succeed. The Japanese army knew that frontal attacks were not easy to invade, so they changed their strategy and again used aircraft and artillery to continuously bombard and explode our outer positions. The artillery fire and bombs were extremely fierce. The positions we built outside the pass were almost completely destroyed. At the same time, Japanese puppet infantry used smoke bombs to cover their attacks on our two wings, attacking our rear. Our garrison outside the pass, fearing being surrounded, had no choice but to abandon the positions outside the pass, retreat to the Lengkou pass, and set up defenses along the Great Wall. On the night of the 10th, more than 1,000 Japanese puppet troops sneaked into the Great Wall through Chenglingkou and advanced to Tuozitou, while some Japanese troops also broke in on the Dongjiakou side and invaded the Shui Lüezhuang and Xiaying area. By dawn on the 11th, battles had taken place in Taipingzhai, Dalingzhai Kou, and Xinzhuang, etc., in the rear of Lengkou. At the same time, the Japanese army on the Lengkou front fiercely bombarded our Lengkou area troops with aircraft and artillery. There were many casualties in the front and rear battles, totaling three days and nights. The rear troops, because of the interference of enemy aircraft and various difficulties, were not easy to reinforce. In addition, the enemy had penetrated deeply and was attacked from both sides. For the sake of gathering forces, Lengkou was temporarily abandoned and retreated to a certain new position. At 11:30 AM that morning, the troops in front of Lengkou retreated one after another, and Jianchangyingzi was also abandoned at the same time. After our army retreated to a new position, the Japanese army continued to advance, and battles also took place near Qian'an. The authorities here urgently transferred a large army to reinforce the area overnight. Today (12th), the reinforcements have arrived, and Shang Zhen ordered a counterattack in the morning, limiting his troops to recover Lengkou within 24 hours. The two sides are currently in fierce fighting.

Since the 9th at dawn, the Luandong aspect, our army launched a full-line counterattack, recaptured Haiyangzhen, and advanced north along the Liujiang Road. The vanguard troops have advanced to the line of the south bank of the Shihe River and the upper and lower Ping Mountains southwest of Shimen Village, as far as Liujiagou. Originally, it could have besieged Shimen and pursued the remnants of the enemy, but because the Japanese army launched a fierce attack on Lengkou Jieling and other places for several consecutive days, our army stopped chasing and stuck to the Tanghe coast for the sake of responding to each other. Since the fall of Lengkou, the Japanese army has penetrated deeply, and Qian'an and Lulong are in a state of emergency at the same time. The situation in Luandong has suddenly become tense. In case of changes in the rear, the armies on the Luandong front will inevitably be affected. At the same time, the Japanese army in the Shimen Village area has also completed its replenishment and has a tendency to invade again. (April 12)

Zhang Boling Talks About the Current Situation in North China, Special Correspondent Geng Ya 103

After the reporter arrived in Tianjin, he immediately visited Mr. Zhang Boling, the president of the Tianjin Local Association. Mr. Zhang suffered from rheumatism in his right arm, but he still received the reporter and had a long conversation. Mr. Zhang immediately took a map and described it orally, roughly saying, "Japanese soldiers continue to occupy our four northeastern provinces without bloodshed, with their heads held high. They originally wanted to invade the Great Wall, intending to invade Chahar and Sui with great force. However, after the unified and courageous resistance of our Song Zheyuan and Shang Zhen's troops, they recaptured several lost key passes, and thus the morale was greatly boosted, and the enemy was also intimidated. Now the defenses around the Great Wall are roughly Gubeikou for the 部 部 troops, Xifengkou for the 部 troops, Lengkou Luanhe Qian'an area for the 部 troops, Zhangjiakou Duolun area for the 部 troops, and Guyuan for the 部 troops. All are strictly disciplined and have the assistance of the local people. Although Tianjin has Japanese troops stationed there due to the Boxer Protocol, the river channel is shallow and easy to silt, making it difficult for warships to enter. Moreover, Mr. Yu Xuezhong's national army has made preparations. If the enemy troops dare to invade, they will be met with strong resistance. The section of the Beining Railway from Tanggu to Linyu is under the threat of Japanese naval artillery fire. Therefore, He Zhuguo's army withdrew from Shimen Village to Luandong, but not because of defeat. Japan also has the Kailuan Mining Company run by the British in the area, fearing to arouse international resentment, so it completely delegated the responsibility of capturing Luandong to the puppet organization Li Jichun's troops. As for Beiping, with Zhang Xueliang's resignation, it seems relatively eased at the moment. It is expected that the center of the future war will gradually shift to Duolun Dushikou and other places, in order to complete the Japanese invasion policy of instigating the Mongolians to establish a "Ancient Map". However, I am afraid that our army in places such as Xifengkou will cut off their retreat, so the Japanese army may advance westward along the Pingyu Avenue, maneuvering and circling with the defenders of our Great Wall. It is also uncertain. We have only three routes to take in response to this serious situation: one is direct negotiation, the second is to recover the lost territory, and the third is to resist to the death. However, given the current bad international situation, even if the government wants to compromise and negotiate, the people will definitely resolutely oppose it. As for recovering the lost territory, we are not sufficiently prepared militarily or economically, so there is no point in talking about it. It is undeniable, so the only grand avenue is to resist desperately. Resist for self-defense, and fight for justice. There will eventually be a day when we win the final victory. Zhang Xueliang's non-resistance in the past, whether it was a merit or a crime, is clear. There is no need to bother saying anything. Tang Yulin disobeyed the order because Wan Fulin disobeyed the order, did not retreat to Chengde, and retreated to Xifengkou, so he also abandoned Chengde, causing him to become the target of public criticism. In fact, those who should be held responsible for the loss of Rehe are not just Tang alone. There are also many people whose crimes are greater than Tang's. These people use the government's vague attitude towards Japan as an excuse to watch and wait, wanting to preserve their strength, and all have plausible arguments. They do not know that foreign aggression is not like internal strife. Preserving strength in internal strife may be possible, but preserving strength when foreign aggression comes and not hesitating to lead thieves into the house will ultimately be abandoned by everyone. On the contrary, if we can embrace the spirit of sacrifice and resolutely resist Japan, we will surely win the sympathy of the people of the country. This is very similar to the meaning of the New Testament saying that 'he who wants to gain his life must lose it.' Due to special political relations, the government is unable to punish derelict soldiers, resulting in the decline of military discipline like a river flowing downhill. If the government can have clear rewards and punishments, not only will such shameless soldiers not be produced in the first place, but the Japanese army will never dare to be so unscrupulous. Now that the government has no clear rewards and punishments, the responsibility of the people is invisibly increased. In other words, for those officers and soldiers who fight bravely and achieve outstanding results on the front lines, they should be given as much assistance as possible in terms of manpower and material resources. Donating money, no matter one yuan or half a mao, can express a great meaning. That is, the joyful donation of each person and each share is no different from casting a most honorary ballot for the heroic soldiers who are fighting for the survival of the nation on the front lines. On the one hand, it can express the enthusiastic sympathy of the people, and on the other hand, it can encourage the courage of the soldiers to thoroughly recognize the anti-imperialist struggle as a glorious war of great value. Furthermore, the compensation and education of the families of the soldiers should be treated even more preferentially than the families of the victims of the civil war, which is reasonable. If the people can uphold justice in this way and hide the profound meaning of encouragement and punishment in the assistance, I know that the brave soldiers will be encouraged to work harder because of this, and the cowardly ones will also know to be cautious because of this, sweeping away the past decadent atmosphere and revitalizing the morale of the new forces. In addition, there are two things that the military and civilians should thoroughly realize: the army must first seek sincere cooperation with the people before it can win outside the border. Tang Yulin's army usually accumulated resentment among the people through bad governance, leading to the great disaster of losing land and harming the country. This is the recent lesson. Furthermore, the most common problem among Chinese people is that they always pursue false fame and do not seek reality. As a result, they often fail to succeed in anything. I hope that all Chinese people will unite to cure this disease. The future of the country and the nation will be almost certain."

Impeachment of Wei Daoming Case (Continued) 104

Enumerating the facts of bribery and illegal acts

Please ask the government to impose disciplinary action according to law

Review Report 105

Regarding the review report, it is found that the case of Shao Hongji, a committee member, impeaching Wei Daoming, the former mayor of Nanjing, for bribery, malfeasance, and dereliction of duty, has been reviewed by the committee members. The review concluded that the bribery was indeed established, the facts were obvious, the dereliction of duty was undeniable, and the impeached person Wei Daoming should be transferred to disciplinary action immediately. The criminal part should be handed over to the court for strict investigation and prosecution, and ordered to be responsible for compensating all losses, in order to warn against corruption and clean up officialdom. Respectfully presented to President Yu, Review Committee members Xiong Yuxi, Zheng Luosheng, Yang Pusheng.

Original Proposal Text 106

Regarding the proposal, it has been found that since the Nanjing Municipal Government of this city discovered that the treasury receipts for collecting housing donations, etc., were forged and there was malfeasance, the entire case has been transferred to the Jiangning District Court for investigation, which has caused considerable suspicion. The capital is located in the capital, and it is urgent to thoroughly investigate it in order to clarify the truth. The committee members immediately went to the Municipal Government, Jiangning District Court, and the citizens to conduct open and secret investigations. It is now found that the Municipal Finance Bureau used three-part receipts to collect various donations in the past. After Mayor Wei Daoming took office, he abolished the three-part receipts and changed to the current two-part treasury receipts of the Municipal Finance Bureau to collect various donations. The receipts were stamped by the Citizen Bank and used to collect housing donations, shop donations, and vehicle donations from the citizens. This was intended to prevent malfeasance by collection personnel, which was indeed a good law and a good intention. Unexpectedly, the opposite was true. Since the use of the two-part treasury receipts, it has indeed been a way to deceive the people of the city with treasury receipts, and to create a large-scale malfeasance case with organization and planning, with those above and below engaging in collusion. If the interior is not leaked, outsiders will never know. Now, if the municipal authorities are willing to collude in malfeasance, this case will never be exposed. Only the details of the forgery of receipts and malfeasance obtained from the investigation are described as follows: (A) Regarding the forgery of treasury receipts, it has been found that the treasury receipts were originally entrusted by the Municipal Government to a printing bureau in Nanjing to be printed in Shanghai, and then sent by the Municipal Government to the Citizen Bank to be stamped, and then used to collect various donations from the citizens. The forged treasury receipts were probably copied and printed by the original printing person who was entrusted. The genuine and fake are slightly different, and it is not easy for outsiders to identify. Moreover, fake bank seals are also forged and stamped on them, or fake seals are used to stamp genuine receipts. On the one hand, fake receipts are used to collect donations, and on the other hand, fake receipts are used to replace genuine receipts. Then, the genuine receipt stubs are used to replace the fake receipt stubs for reporting, or the fake receipt stubs are used to replace the genuine receipt stubs for reporting. There are about a dozen types of malfeasance methods. In short, fake is mixed with genuine, and genuine is mixed with fake, trying to do everything possible to commit malfeasance. The city needs about 60,000 treasury receipts every month. If the number of forgeries is estimated at 20% of the lowest number, about 12,000 fake receipts are used every month. If each receipt is estimated to have a minimum of two yuan of malfeasance, about 28,000 yuan is embezzled every month, which is already alarming, but I am afraid that it is more than this number. This relates to the situation of forgery and malfeasance. (B) Regarding the malfeasance of collection personnel, it has been found that the municipal revenue of this city is mainly from housing donations. There is no proportion of how much is collected every month, and there is no statistics every year. The collection personnel are allowed to fabricate reports at will, as much or as little as they want. With such a large revenue, how could the municipal authorities in the past have been deaf and blind, and turn a deaf ear to it? This can prove the reason for collusion between those above and below. Also, it has been found that there are about 50 collection personnel in the Municipal Finance Bureau, who hold treasury receipts to collect housing donations, shop donations, or vehicle donations from citizens every month. Some give fake receipts, and some give genuine receipts. For example, if the first collector issues a fake receipt to the citizen, the second collector will not collect if he sees a fake receipt, or if the first collector issues a genuine receipt to the citizen, the second collector will not collect if he sees that it has already been collected. Moreover, the receipts are not signed or stamped, which is clear evidence of the collusion of collection personnel. Furthermore, the receipt stubs of the treasury receipts returned by the collection personnel are mixed with genuine and fake ones, the numbers are disordered, and there is no report of the number of receipts received and spent, and the remaining number, nor is there a report form for the amount of money collected. However, the person who issues and receives the receipts and the accountant have never raised any objections. Even the audit department of the Municipal Government has not found a single forged receipt. This receipt has passed through the hands of more than a dozen people from the time it was issued and returned to the time it was audited and filed, for several years, and no one has been heard to know and report it. This is clear evidence of the collusion of those above and below in committing malfeasance, without any doubt. From this, it can be known that it is an organized, planned, and entire large-scale malfeasance case, which is not an exaggeration. Based on the above facts, if the mayors and finance directors in the past were unaware, how could the audit personnel of the municipal government and all the relevant collection staff of the finance bureau dare to commit malfeasance for three years, embezzling public funds of about one million yuan, until it was discovered last month? Although the municipal government has handed over the personnel involved in the collection and use of fake receipts to the court for trial, it has failed to thoroughly investigate the principal offenders, which is not in accordance with the fairness of the law. Also, it has been found that Wei Hanqing, an official in the finance bureau in charge of treasury receipts during Mayor Wei's tenure, reported the loss of 82 waste tickets for 100 yuan shops, 507 waste tickets for 10 yuan shops, 15 waste tickets for 100 yuan households, and 300 waste tickets for 10 yuan households, totaling 904 tickets, with a face value of 17,770 yuan. He did not check the starting and ending numbers of the lost tickets, but vaguely reported them, which was obviously to reserve a place for future malfeasance. The mayor knew this but did not investigate it, nor did he announce it or publish a statement in the newspaper to declare it invalid, but simply approved it in one batch. The hidden situation is self-evident. It has been proven by the court's investigation of this lost ticket that it has now been found on the market collecting donations, which is sufficient to prove that Wei Daoming is undoubtedly the principal offender in condoning malfeasance and forging official documents and seals. All the former mayors Wei Daoming and the former finance directors Qi Xu, Wang Renlin, and Cheng Yuanfan, etc., are not only derelict in their duties, but are in fact colluding in malfeasance, which is unforgivable by law. Therefore, I hereby impeach them in accordance with the law and request that Wei Daoming, Qi Xu, Wang Renlin, Cheng Yuanfan, and Wei Hanqing, etc., be transferred to disciplinary action immediately, and request that the embezzled public funds be strictly recovered, and that the relevant criminal part be immediately handed over to the court for trial, in order to emphasize the rule of law and rectify officialdom. This is presented to the President for review and implementation, Shao Hongji, Supervisor.

Review Report 107

Regarding the review report, the case of Committee Member Shao Hongji impeaching Wei Daoming, the former mayor of Nanjing, and the former finance directors Qi Xu, Wang Renlin, Cheng Yuanfan, etc., for forging receipts and embezzling money has been handed over to the committee members for review. The committee members have reviewed it in detail and all agree that the Municipal Government of this city discovered that there were forgeries and malfeasance in the treasury receipts for collecting housing donations, etc. The genuine and fake receipts have been kept in the court for investigation and prosecution. Furthermore, Committee Member Shao personally investigated and found that the number of forgeries has not been determined, but even if calculated at the lowest limit, the amount of floating receipts every month is about 28,000 yuan, and those above and below have been deceiving each other for three years. As the city government agency in the capital, a major malfeasance case has occurred, and it is necessary to investigate its responsibility thoroughly. Although the municipal government has handed over the relevant people involved in the collection of receipts to the court for trial, the people in charge at the time, even if they were the principal offenders in malfeasance and forging official documents and seals, have been allowed to go unpunished, which is not in accordance with the fairness of the law. It is requested that the impeached former mayor Wei Daoming, former finance directors Qi Xu, Wang Renlin, Cheng Yuanfan, and the treasury receipt official Wei Hanqing be handed over to disciplinary action immediately, and that the relevant criminal part be transferred to the court for trial, in order to clear up the accumulated malpractices and warn against future evils. This report is respectfully submitted to President Yu, Supervisor Yang Tianji, He Jiwu, Li Shijun.

Songjiang

County Administration Conference Minutes 109

Yesterday, the county government held its 201st county administration conference, chaired by County Magistrate Jin. The matters discussed were: (1) The case of storing two or three months of food rations as ordered, and how to formulate a method for raising funds and storing food rations. It was resolved that: (a) a letter should be sent to the Food Ration Committee to report the current situation of distributing rice for disaster relief and the exact number of rice stored for overall planning; (b) the number of rice owed for disaster relief should be strictly pursued from each district; (c) a county-wide grain storage conference should be convened on a fixed date; (2) The Property Division requested that the 2% agricultural fee collected with the mining tax be transferred to this division for collection. It was resolved that the matter be left for the next meeting. (3) The county government proposed that Wang Lie of the Shanghai Bee Farm present a request for protection for raising Italian bees in the county. It was resolved that a specific area should be designated for a trial basis. Other cases were omitted.

Suzhou

People Allowed to Accuse Corrupt Local Tyrants 110

Zou Xiaogong, the administrative inspector of the Third District of Jiangsu, issued a proclamation on the 14th to Changshu, Kunshan, and Wujiang counties. The main idea of the proclamation is that if there are corrupt local tyrants who disrupt local public security, the people are allowed to accuse them according to law. Once verified, they will be severely punished according to law without pardon. He also instructed the county magistrates not to accept bribes or engage in malfeasance.

Chamber of Commerce Strives for Telephone Deposit Fee 111

The Wuxian Chamber of Commerce considered the additional deposit fee charged by the Suzhou Telephone Bureau to be illegal. It had submitted a request to the Ministry of Communications, requesting the Ministry to order the Suzhou Telephone Bureau to correct it and reduce the burden on merchants. Subsequently, the Ministry approved the request. Yesterday, the Chamber of Commerce submitted the case to a joint executive and supervisory meeting for deliberation. It was decided that the deposit fee should be 20 yuan. Those who have paid will not be increased, and those who have not paid in full will be required to pay the difference. The case will be submitted to the Ministry of Communications for approval and implementation.

Wuxi

Villagers Demolish the Defense Corps Headquarters 112

Villagers of Gangxia Township, the seventh district under this county, had pooled funds to perform a Tanhuang opera about ten days ago and hired a famous Tanhuang troupe to perform in the village. Having obtained the consent of the township head, who also served as the head of the Defense Corps, they began the performance, which lasted for two days. However, the squad leader of the Defense Corps, believing that it was detrimental to public morals and indirectly involved gambling and harboring bandits, strongly advocated for its prohibition. The head of the corps, feeling constrained by public opinion, had no choice but to order the performance to stop. This caused a group of villagers to resent the Defense Corps squad leader and call for revenge. Soon, over a thousand people gathered within an hour. Among them was Zang Xing, who ran a teahouse, who declared they should take up arms. So, everyone took up hoes, rakes, and clubs as weapons and stormed the Defense Corps. They tore up all the documents, letters, and uniforms, and even seized firearms. Several militiamen were beaten and injured. Afterwards, militiamen from the Defense Corps arrested two villagers, Sun Lvkang and Sun Shunjin, who were involved in the violence, intending to take them to the city for legal proceedings. However, the township head mediated between the two sides, ordering Zang Xing and Sun Lvkang, etc., to raise 328 yuan to compensate the Defense Corps for the losses. The lost firearms were also recovered from the river and returned to the corps headquarters.

Bandits Rob Two Pig Boats in Succession 113

Hua Afa, a resident of Liuxiang, Zhangjing Township, the fifth district in the north (Tianshang City) of this county, makes a living by steering pig boats. The other day, at dusk, Liu Afa's pig boat and Wang Laowu's pig boat, from Jiangbei, were both loading pigs in Jiangbei to come to Xixi. They anchored in Zhangjing Creek overnight. Unexpectedly, in the middle of the night, four or five bandit boats suddenly came. More than ten bandits swarmed aboard, tied up the owners and crew of the two pig boats, and robbed them of more than 70 yuan in cash and 38 large pigs. After the bandits had plundered enough, they set sail and fled. Afterwards, Yang Zuxun, the head of the fourth Jia of the Sitou Town Defense Corps in the district, led militiamen and intercepted two bandit boats at the No. 3 Bridge on the Xicheng Road. They found 13 large pigs in the boats and arrested a deaf-mute suspect. They presented these all together to the Fifth District Corps Headquarters and yesterday submitted a written report to the county government for review.

Xue Congfu, the head of the County Water Patrol Team, has been in office for a year and a half without much achievement. The new County Magistrate, Wang ShengGao, has appointed He Linchun to take over as the team leader. He arrived at the county on the 11th to take over the duties.

Defense Corps Captures a Large Number of Stolen Goods and Thieves 115

The Zoumatang Defense Corps in the ninth district of Wuyi recently received a tip-off that a large number of bandits were gathering and dispersing irregularly in the vicinity and had committed robberies in several households. They immediately dispatched teams to search in all directions. On the 11th and 12th, they successively captured a number of bandits, including Yang Genfa, Ma Yinpei, Hou Bingli, and Guan A'da, in Pangjia Street and other places, along with two rifles, seven bullets, and five bundles of clothing totaling 118 pieces. Another bandit, Ma Jinlin, drowned while trying to escape by swimming when being captured. Hu Fengshan, the captain of the Zhenjiang County Government Police Brigade, was transferred here from Pi County last spring and has served for more than a year. The Zhenjiang County Agricultural Experiment Station is handling the planting of roadside trees on the third section of Zhongzheng Road and Jingji Road in the provincial capital. The work has now been completed and a request has been submitted to the Zhenjiang County Government to forward it to the Department of Construction for inspection. After receiving the report, the Department of Construction has sent Xie Mingke, a forestry technician from the department, to inspect and accept the work.

Silkworm Seeds are Printed with Labels 118

The Jiangsu Department of Construction previously received a report from the Provincial Silkworm Industry Regulation Office stating that there have been reports of qualified certificates issued to various seed production sites being misused by others in the past. To prevent problems from arising, it is proposed that the qualified certificates issued this year should not only be printed with the words "Jiangsu Year 22 Spring Stable", but also be printed with separate labels on the qualified certificates for ordinary seeds or original silkworm seeds used by each site, so that each site cannot misuse them to prevent abuses. The Department of Construction now considers the proposed measures to be feasible and has approved them for record.

Fan Hengsheng, a notorious bandit from the northern countryside, has recently led a group to commit robberies in over a hundred cases, killing many victims. Most recently, he robbed the Sun family in Banqiao in the southern countryside and killed three people. Wang Talks About No Direct Contact Between China and Japan

Negotiating While Resisting

Wang Jingwei, the President of the Executive Yuan, together with his wife, Ms. Chen Bijun, and the Ministry of Railways

Departed from Beijing by night train and arrived in Shanghai. Mr. Wang visited Song Ziwen twice yesterday to urge him to

Talks. As a result, Song has already agreed in person and will set sail for the United States within the next few days. As for Song's

Financial issues have been largely decided to be handled by Zhang Shuyong, Financial Advisor, and Financial Secretary

The situation is recorded as follows:

Visit to Song Ziwen 121

Wang Jingwei, President of the Executive Yuan, and his wife, together with Zeng Zhongming, Vice Minister of the Ministry of Railways, arrived in Shanghai from Beijing by overnight express train at about 11:00 p.m. and arrived at Zhenru Station at 7:40 a.m. yesterday. Before leaving Beijing, President Wang had telegraphed Finance Minister Song Ziwen to come to Shanghai to discuss the matter of attending the Washington Economic Conference in person. Therefore, Mr. Song sent Tang Haian, the Jianghai Customs Supervisor, to Zhenru Station to welcome Mr. Wang yesterday morning, and they went to visit Song on Qiqi Road in the same car. Wang's wife, Ms. Chen Bijun, and Mr. Zeng Zhongming took their own cars and returned to Wang's residence on Pushi Road. After Wang and others arrived at Song's residence, they met with Song Ziwen. Wang earnestly requested Mr. Song to serve as our country's representative to attend the Washington Economic Conference. Mr. Song initially declined and suggested Sun Ke instead. After Mr. Wang explained that Sun Min is currently tied up with the work of the Legislative Yuan and cannot leave, and that Mr. Song has been in charge of finance for many years and is more suitable, and that all parties have high expectations for Song, he asked Song to reluctantly take on the difficult task. Soon, Xu Mo, the Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs, also arrived. The three gentlemen talked for a long time, and Song agreed to consider it before making a decision. At 9:35, Wang and Xu left one after another. By 4:30 yesterday afternoon, Wang borrowed the residence of Li Shizeng, a member of the Central Committee, and visited Song's residence again to continue discussing the issue of attendance. The three gentlemen talked for about two hours, and Song finally agreed to serve as a representative. It was also largely decided that after Song leaves the country, the military expenses and financial issues in North China will be temporarily managed by Zhang Shuyong, a senior advisor to the Ministry of Finance, and Li Tiaosheng and Zou Lin, the financial secretaries. Wang and Li left at 6:20 p.m.

Going Abroad in a Few Days 122

As a result of the consultation between Wang and Song, Mr. Song decided to leave Shanghai to go abroad within the next few days. Those traveling with him will probably be Dr. Yang Ge, the American advisor to the Ministry of Finance, and a few secretaries. Because Mr. Song considered the domestic financial issues to be extremely important after he left Shanghai, he invited Zhang Shuyong to meet at Song's residence at 5:30 yesterday afternoon. The two gentlemen talked until about 7:00 p.m. before leaving.

Wang's Talk 123

At 10:30 yesterday morning, our reporter visited Wang Jingwei at his residence. According to Wang, the purpose of his trip to Shanghai was entirely to urge Minister Song Ziwen to represent our country to go to the United States to attend the Washington Conference, because this Washington Conference is of great importance. All countries in the world have sent first-class figures to participate, such as British Prime Minister MacDonald and French former Prime Minister Herriot. Therefore, the choice of our country's candidates should be particularly careful. The Central Committee originally planned to choose one of the two gentlemen, Finance Minister Song Ziwen and Legislative Yuan President Sun Ke, to attend. However, Mr. Sun is the President of the Legislative Yuan, and the organizational law of the Provisional National Congress, the election law of the National Congress, and the draft constitution must be formulated before July 1st. Therefore, no matter what, he cannot get away, let alone go abroad. The Central Committee then decided to invite Song to go, and because Song is our country's financial authority and is familiar with the world's economic situation, this position is even more suitable. However, at this time of national crisis, the raising of military expenses in North China and other financial issues are also extremely important. If Mr. Song can make the trip, he should make considerable preparations before leaving the country. I met with Mr. Song this morning, and I will visit him again in the afternoon. A final decision can be made tonight (that is, last night). I will return to Beijing the same night or tomorrow after Mr. Song agrees in person.

Issue of Political Prisoners 124

Wang then talked about the issue of opening up political rights, saying that Ms. Song Qingling, Mrs. Sun, came to Beijing last time as a representative of the China League for Civil Rights to request two points from the government: (1) Release all political prisoners in the country; (2) Abolish the singular law. I met with Mrs. Sun in person at that time, explained in detail, and repeatedly stated in a long letter that the main point is that regarding the first point, the Central Committee convened the Second Plenary Session last year and discussed this issue, and the National Crisis Conference has already gathered people from all walks of life with different political views to participate in the discussion together, and in fact they have all been pardoned. Therefore, there are no so-called political prisoners in prison now. If there are any, they are the communists who have been arrested in the past. The communists are now causing trouble everywhere and plotting to subvert the country, so they cannot be treated the same as ordinary political prisoners. As for what is meant by abolishing the singular law, it refers to the Law on Punishing Crimes Endangering the Republic of China in Emergency Situations. This article is also specifically designed for the communists today. Just look at the countries in Europe and America. Because the communists do not have riots and other situations, there are regulations on freedom of speech and publication. However, the situation of the communists in China today has gone beyond the scope of riots, so how can they be compared with other countries?

Southwest Decides to Send Troops 125

The reporter then asked President Wang about the issue of sending troops from the Southwest to resist Japan and suppress bandits. According to Wang, I met with Yang Dezhao, the representative of Chen Jitang, yesterday and learned that the Southwest is still proceeding with the original plan to send troops to resist Japan and suppress communists. Some people in Guangdong are opposed to the Provisional National Congress because of misunderstandings, which have been explained by the Central Committee in a telegram. I have not heard of the rumor that the Central Committee will send Minister Huang to Hong Kong to explain the matter. After Chiang, the chairman, personally went to supervise the suppression of bandits in Jiangxi, the bandit forces have been slightly weakened. After Chairman Chiang has properly deployed the military to suppress bandits, he will go north to command the resistance against Japan.

Public Remarks 126

Wang also made public remarks at the same time: Question: There have been many rumors about Sino-Japanese compromise recently. What is the truth? Answer: Indeed, there are rumors, but I believe that people with common sense can easily judge what is a rumor and what is a fact. May I ask how China and Japan can compromise? Will Japan abandon its aggressive acts in the three northeastern provinces and Rehe, and abolish the puppet government of Manchuria? Does China recognize Japan's aggressive acts in the three northeastern provinces and Rehe, and recognize the puppet government of Manchuria? Since Japan is unwilling to do the former and China is unwilling to do the latter, may I ask how can they compromise? Question: You advocate that resistance and negotiation should be carried out at the same time. Are you still adhering to this policy now? Answer: I am still adhering to this policy. First, let's talk about resistance. We certainly cannot say that we are sure of victory, but we must do our best to resist. This can be said with certainty. Since Chairman Chiang went north to supervise the military in North China and the generals of all armies are united in resisting the enemy, although we cannot say that there has been great progress, it is stronger than the Battle of Rehe. This is a fact that can be proven. We are determined to resist and do our best to resist. We do not exaggerate small victories and do not become discouraged by temporary failures. Only in this way can we achieve the goal of long-term resistance. Second, let's talk about negotiation. Recently, the League of Nations has made a resolution to impose moral sanctions on Japan. Military sanctions may not be able to be determined for a while in fact, but they are a natural step in principle. If not, moral sanctions will become empty words. Speaking of rumors just now, I am reminded of one thing. Have you seen the recent arguments in Japanese newspapers? They say that China is still actively resisting Japan and that Japan must attack Guan Nei. Comparing this argument with the so-called rumors makes people feel very emotional. I advise the people to pay attention to the arguments in the Japanese media rather than paying attention to rumors, so that they can have a clearer understanding of the other party. I would also like to say that not all Japanese people support the invasion of China. The most correct argument is that if this invasion continues, it will lead to "the common demise of China and Japan." How earnest are their words! I believe that today, in addition to resistance, we must awaken all countries in the world to impose strong sanctions on Japan's aggressive actions, and we must also awaken the powerful forces in Japan to stop their own aggressive actions. This is the effort we should make. Question: Recently, there have been rumors that the government is unwilling to fully accommodate opinions from all parties on the major policies of peace and war, resulting in many misunderstandings. Even the central committee members and military committee members have such arguments. What is the actual situation? Answer: The national crisis is so serious that speaking of war, there is the danger of losing soldiers and land; speaking of peace, there is the danger of losing power and humiliating the country; speaking of neither peace nor war, there is danger in both. Therefore, the people who are currently in Nanjing politics are as anxious as if they are throwing themselves into a fire pit. We are determined to go to the country's difficulties together and jump into the fire pit. At the same time, we are only grateful and motivated when we see people jumping into the fire pit together. There is no reason to reject them. All kinds of conferences are now sincerely inviting people who should attend and attend to come to attend. In other words, we are sincerely inviting comrades to jump into the fire pit together. If some of the comrades cannot come due to job responsibilities, and communication cannot be fully clarified, resulting in misunderstandings, we are very sorry and will only try to remedy these shortcomings. We will never believe that in this time of national peril, there will still be people standing far away outside the fire pit, making sarcastic remarks. If there are, we have no choice, but we must know that if the Nanjing government collapses, it is not the collapse of one person, but the collapse of the entire government. If you think that after the Nanjing government collapses, you can still maintain half of the country in the Northwest, Southwest, and Southeast (not to mention the Northeast because the Northeast is gone), I am afraid there is no such good dream. As far as I am concerned, before the September 18th Incident, I disagreed with many comrades in Nanjing because of the promotion of policies. But after the September 18th Incident, I only buried my head and jumped into the fire pit. I have recently returned, not because I am confident in saving the country, but because I think that at least jumping into the fire pit will allow me to die at ease.

Shanghai Telephone Bureau Will Switch to Automatic Telephones Today 132

And Increase the Number of Concession Lines by Eleven Pairs

Convenient for All City Users, No Increase in Fees

The Shanghai Telephone Bureau's automatic telephone has been installed and will officially start operation at 12:00 midnight on the 15th of this month. Communication lines have been improved and increased for communication between the Nanshi, Zhabei, and Concession areas. The details are as follows:

Official Operation 133

The Telephone Bureau announced that the automatic telephone was being upgraded and installed. Three years have passed, and the project has been delayed many times due to various factors. Now, in compliance with the Ministry's order, we have urged the progress and have completed all work in the Nanshi and Zhabei districts. It is scheduled to officially open communication at 12:00 midnight on the 15th of this month. Before 12:00, users must still report their numbers as before. After 12:00, they can use the converter. During the transition between the old and new systems, there may be some obstacles. Please be kind and considerate. In addition, users should prepare a new phone book and bring the notification issued by the bureau with the official seal before 12:00 noon on the 15th to the bureau to collect it. This is to notify you.

Increase in Communication Lines 134

A reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency met with Xu Xueyu, the director of the telephone bureau. According to him, the automatic telephone will officially start operation at 12:00 midnight on the 15th. At the same time, communication lines will be increased. For example, from Nanshi to Zhabei, the original 19 pairs of lines were rented from the Concession Telephone Company, with each pair costing 50 taels. In view of the fact that communication was insufficient during communication, for the convenience of citizens, a consultation was held with the Concession Telephone Company, and it was decided that starting from the 15th, the number of lines will be increased to 30 pairs, and the rental fee for each pair will increase from 50 taels to 200 taels. At that time, there will be no sense of insufficient application.

Concession Communication 135

As for communication with the concession, users originally had to notify the Shanghai Telephone Bureau's manual operator, and then the manual operator would notify the Concession Telephone Company's manual operator to transfer to the user. The procedure was cumbersome and would inevitably take a long time. For the sake of speed, it has been decided that when the automatic machine is in communication, users will notify the telephone bureau's manual operator, and the manual operator will directly transfer to the user. At the same time, the original 19 pairs of telephone lines will be increased to 30 pairs. A deposit of 5 yuan will still be required in advance, and the fee will be 5 cents per three minutes.

Switchboard Operators 136

The Shanghai Telephone Bureau has more than 140 male and female switchboard operators. After the automatic machine is used, it is inevitable that the number of operators will be reduced. It has now been decided to re-employ the best operators based on their performance, character, and length of service by means of an examination, about 100 of them. The bureau will be responsible for recommending the rest to telephone bureaus in the interior for employment.

Foreign Ships Obey the Regulations and Inspection 137

Regarding the inspection of foreign ships, according to the person in charge of the Maritime Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation, in the past, foreign ships entering the country often failed to obey Chinese laws and regulations for inspection. Later, personnel were sent to explain to various foreign shipping companies and provide guidance, and now more and more ships are obeying the regulations and coming to the bureau for inspection. The inspection procedures are exactly the same as those for domestic ships. After inspection, the bureau will issue a temporary or regular inspection certificate to each ship. After receiving the inspection certificate, each ship can enter the port and pass through.

Chen Taosheng Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday to Study Brewing in Europe and the United States 139

Chen Taosheng (Taoxin), a technician of the Ministry of Industry and a technical commissioner of the Central Industrial Testing Institute, was dispatched to the United States in January last year to study sugar production and brewing. After arriving in the United States, he entered the Graduate School of Louisiana State University in the southern United States to study sugar production. In his spare time, he also practiced in the private laboratory of Dr. Owen, a brewing professor. The completed theses include "Microbial Research on Chinese Brewing Products" and "Fermentation Experiment of Cuban Molasses," which were published in famous American magazines. In November, after being awarded a master's degree in sugar production by Louisiana State University, he went to the Graduate School of the University of Wisconsin in the northern United States to study fermentation microbiology and fermentation chemistry. In mid-January of this year, he went to Chicago, Washington, and New York to visit government research institutions. In early February, he went to Europe from New York, stayed in Europe for a month, and visited more than 20 academic institutions and famous factories in the United Kingdom, Germany, France, and the Netherlands. He visited almost all sugar production and brewing experts in Europe and the United States and brought back many works and publications. Yesterday, he arrived in Shanghai. He told visitors that China is oppressed by world science, which has led to the shrinking of its territory and the poverty of its people. From now on, if we want to consolidate national defense and develop industry, we must promote science. The Ministry of Industry is responsible for developing the national industry and should immediately concentrate national talents in the capital to imitate foreign goods and investigate domestic products in order to study established methods and detailed plans to show the people, and the results will be significant. As for the setting of tariffs, the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry should earnestly consult to prevent domestic products from being hit by foreign goods. The Department of Agriculture and the Department of Commerce in the United States are called government offices, but they are actually the most complete research institutions. Our country should take this as a model. The scientific organization of the Ministry of Industry is an imminent task, and the industrial institutions in various provinces should also focus on researching local products and promoting local industries. Everyone should break the idea of being an official and do practical work, so that the country can have hope. It is said that before Mr. Chen went abroad,

French Female Aviator Hilze Arrived in Shanghai from Hong Kong Yesterday 140

Flying to Seoul This Morning and Transferring to Tokyo

French female aviator Hilze, accompanied by engineer Lemoire, flew from Paris, the capital of France, on the 1st of this month, piloting a 300-horsepower monoplane, the F-A1ui, on a long-distance flight. After passing through Italy, Brandisi Greece, Athens, Arabia, Aleppo, India, Hong Kong, and other places, they arrived in Shanghai at 3 p.m. yesterday and are scheduled to leave Shanghai at 6 a.m. this morning to fly to Seoul and transfer to Tokyo. The details of their arrival in Shanghai are recorded as follows:

Arriving in Shanghai at 3 PM 141

The F-Alui single-wing aircraft, piloted by the lady, has 300 horsepower. Furthermore, the aircraft was manufactured only two months ago, so the flight was swift. It departed from Hong Kong at 6:30 AM yesterday, scheduled to arrive at Hongqiao Airport at 12:30 PM. However, due to heavy fog and strong winds yesterday, the speed of the flight was greatly reduced, and it didn't land at Hongqiao Airport until 3 PM.

Welcoming Personnel 142

The French Consul General in Shanghai, Mr. Mérey, Vice-Consul Mr. Gouffre, and more than 30 French nationals, arrived at the airport one after another around 11 AM yesterday to welcome her. Our side also sent Mr. Zhong Ziliang, Secretary of the China Aviation Association, to welcome her. The French Concession Police Political Department and the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau both dispatched personnel to provide security. The Foreign Affairs Section of the Public Security Bureau specifically sent Chen Shoujing, Zhang Feifan, and others to the scene to check passports and other documents because a foreign aircraft was entering.

Disembarkation 143

After the plane landed, all the welcoming personnel present approached the aircraft. Consul General Mérey personally assisted the lady in disembarking. Despite only wearing a single layer of clothing after the long flight, she was covered in sweat. After Mr. Mérey and others expressed their welcome, Mr. Zhong Ziliang, our representative, also stepped forward with a bouquet of flowers to pay his respects. Immediately afterward, they went into the airport office, where the lady signed a type of arrival diary and filled out the inspection form of our Public Security Bureau. Once everything was completed, she went with the welcoming personnel in several cars to the thirteen-story building on Avenue Petain to rest. That night, she attended a welcome banquet hosted by the French community at the same building.

The Lady's Speech 144

After the lady disembarked, she thanked the welcomers and then gave a brief speech to the Chinese and foreign reporters at the airport, saying, "I took off from Hong Kong at 6:30 this morning. Because I encountered strong winds and heavy fog along the way, it took eight hours and thirty minutes to reach Shanghai. I will not stay in Shanghai for long. If the weather is clear tomorrow (i.e., today), I have decided to fly to Seoul at 6 AM, and then go on to Tokyo." The lady is thirty years old, exceptionally healthy and beautiful, and often gives a slight smile when speaking to people.

Photography Detained 145

After the news of the lady's flight from Hong Kong to Shanghai spread, reporters from Chinese and foreign newspapers in Shanghai rushed to the airport to gather news. Japanese reporters Mr. Tashiro Masao and Mr. Koji Okeyl from the Shanghai Mainichi Shimbun also entered the airport with cameras. Unexpectedly, the Japanese reporters did not listen to the warnings of our soldiers protecting the airport and repeatedly secretly photographed the airport fortress. Our military officers, because they repeatedly warned them without success, recorded their names and detained the photos they had taken. The foreigners present also mocked and ridiculed the Japanese for secretly photographing the fortress.

The Ministry of Communications Approved the Extraterritorial Telephone Contract for Signing 148

Director Xu Negotiated with the Telephone Company Yesterday

The Original Text Will Be Officially Announced After Signing

The draft contract for the extraterritorial road construction telephone has been approved by the Ministry of Communications. Director Xu negotiated with the Concession Telephone Company yesterday and decided to officially sign it on the 18th. The details are recorded as follows:

Ministry Order Approved: Xu Xueyu, Director of the Shanghai Telephone Bureau, submitted a draft contract to the Ministry of Communications regarding the extraterritorial road construction telephone to be signed with the Concession Telephone Company. On the 10th of this month, he went to Beijing and requested instructions from Zhu Jiahao, Minister of Communications. In order to facilitate the speedy resolution for the convenience of citizens, the Ministry approved the draft. Mr. Xu returned to Shanghai from Beijing on the evening of the 12th, and the approval order arrived in Shanghai on the 13th.

Scheduled Signing: After the Shanghai Telephone Bureau received the Ministry's approval order, it immediately formally wrote to the Concession Telephone Company, expressing its agreement. Penalties for Fishery Construction Fees 152

The Fishery Improvement Committee of the Ministry of Industries' Jiangsu and Zhejiang Region Fishery Construction Fee Collection Office issued a notice stating: "Regarding the issuance of a notice, we have received Order No. 1 from the Fishery Improvement Committee of the Ministry of Industries' Jiangsu and Zhejiang Region, which states, 'We hereby appoint Committee Member Dai Yongtang concurrently as Director of the Fishery Construction Fee Collection Office, this order,' etc., and a seal is issued. Upon receiving this order, in addition to taking office and using the seal on a selected day and submitting separate letters, we should earnestly comply with the resolutions of the temporary meeting of the Fishery Improvement Committee of the Ministry of Industries' Jiangsu and Zhejiang Region, which decided that the Fishery Construction Fee will be collected starting from April 15, and the rate of 1% will be temporarily collected based on 2%, etc." It is hereby announced to make it known. "It has been found that the Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces are vast, and in order to avoid being beyond reach, the office has divided the area into ten districts according to regulations. In addition to the Songhu District, which is concurrently managed by the office and no separate branch will be established, nine branches have been designated, including the Ningzhen District, Ding Shen District, Ningxiang South District, Wentai District, Hangjiashao District, Hutaisu District, Chongtong District, Haizhou District, and Jingchang District. All fresh, salted, dried, and shellfish fishery products will be subject to a fishery construction fee of 1% of the value, starting from April 15. Merchants in various places are responsible for collecting the fee on behalf of the office according to the price. It should be known that this fishery construction fee has been approved by the Central Political Council and is purely based on the principle of taking it from fisheries and using it for fisheries. It is completely different in nature from fishery tax. At a time when fisheries are declining, improving fisheries is urgent. All fishery personnel should fulfill their obligation to pay a small fee and give the fisheries a huge construction, and should understand the government's intention to improve fisheries and earnestly comply with the requirements. If there is any deliberate delay or intention to evade, once discovered, they will be punished according to the regulations. The penalties are listed below. It is hereby announced to make it widely known. The penalties are as follows: Article 1. These penalties are formulated in accordance with Article 7 of the Provisional Regulations on the Collection of Fishery Construction Fees by the Fishery Improvement Committee of the Ministry of Industries' Jiangsu and Zhejiang Region. Article 2. Anyone who transports fishery products with less reporting or evasion will be ordered to make up the construction fee and will be fined five to fifteen times the amount of the unreported fee. Article 3. Anyone who fails to comply with or refuses the inspection of the inspectors will be ordered to comply with the procedures, and after verification, will be fined 10 to 50 yuan. Article 4. Anyone who forges or alters fishery construction fee receipts will be punished in accordance with the law on forging valuable securities. Article 5. Any fishery personnel who violate more than two articles of these penalties will be punished separately in accordance with the provisions of each article. Article 6. The aforementioned fines shall be filled out by the punishing authority with the actual amount of the penalty on four-part penalty slips, which shall be issued separately and reported to the Ministry. The aforementioned four-part penalty slips shall be printed and issued by the Fishery Improvement Committee of the Ministry of Industries' Jiangsu and Zhejiang Region, and the collection agency shall affix a seal. Article 7. Seventy percent of the aforementioned fines shall be confiscated, and thirty percent shall be awarded to the person who discovered and reported the violation. The confiscated funds shall be remitted by the collection agency to the Fishery Improvement Committee of the Ministry of Industries' Jiangsu and Zhejiang Region for safekeeping at the end of each month. Article 8. These penalties shall be implemented from the date of promulgation. April 8, 22nd year of the Republic of China, Director Dai Yongtang.
