Grain Prices Falling, Coarse Grain Industry Appeals for Relief 156

Foreign Rice and Wheat Flour Dumped Domestically

Requesting the Central Government to Impose Heavy Taxes

The Coarse Grain Industry Association submitted a document to the Municipal Party Department, the Bureau of Social Affairs, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday, requesting that it be forwarded to the central government, stating, "Regarding the dumping of imported foreign rice and wheat flour, which harms our country's agricultural products, we request to impose heavy taxes to benefit the national economy and the people's livelihood. We respectfully ask for your consideration. Our country is vast and rich in resources, and the food produced is sufficient to feed itself. There is no need for foreign goods. Unfortunately, after the disaster of war, we suffered widespread droughts and floods, and the people's food was occasionally panicked. As a result, foreign rice and wheat flour were imported in a continuous stream, and the outflow of money was countless. Fortunately, last year's harvest in the provinces along the Yangtze River made people happy that both farmers and merchants could recover. Unexpectedly, due to the world's overproduction, rice, wheat, and flour were shipped to our country, competing with each other and dumping at lower prices without limit, causing grain prices to plummet and farmers and merchants to suffer. Take rice as an example. The farmers' hard work all year round is not enough to offset the wages and rent taxes. The association's merchants transport goods from the place of origin to Shanghai, and all of them lose money. The rice from Hunan and Jiangxi to Shanghai relies on the purchase and transportation from Fujian Province to barely make a living, but the supply exceeds the demand and it is difficult to reverse the decline. As of now, the current value in this city is that the highest-grade machine-milled white rice from Hunan and Jiangxi is only 8 yuan, 2 or 3 jiao per stone. All external costs, such as麻袋 packing and transportation from the origin to Shanghai, require 2 yuan to 2 yuan and a half per stone. Based on this, the selling price at the place of origin is only about 6 yuan. Converting paddy rice into machine-milled white rice, the bran and grain are consumed by about half, so the farmer's income is only about 2 yuan, 4 or 5 jiao per stone of rice. The cheap grain hurts the farmers to the extreme. It has been found that the two Guangdong provinces are rice-deficient areas, with an annual shortage of about 10 million stone. In terms of relief, last year the five provinces of Hunan, Jiangxi, Anhui, Jiangsu, and Zhejiang had enough surplus rice to provide ample relief, but upon closer examination of the amount of rice purchased and sold in the two Guangdong provinces, only Wuhu had a small amount of transportation, and nineteen were seized by foreign rice. At present, the late rice in Shanghai has a thick accumulation, and the market price is as cheap as mentioned above, and the price of foreign rice is falling further, and there are frequent reports of secret orders. Alas, if this continues, the grain price will plummet, and it is impossible to predict the future. As for the domestic production of wheat, new wheat will be available in two months. Even if the flour mills need to order foreign wheat, they should limit the amount to two months' worth, but the reality is not the case. Various foreign wheat manufacturers in Australia, Canada, and Argentina, because of their low prices, are actively ordering from abroad on the one hand and aggressively selling futures in China on the other hand. In the future, when domestic new wheat is launched on the market, both farmers and merchants will be defeated, and there is no need to wait for tortoises to predict the future. In summary, it can be seen that the affairs of the national economy and the people's livelihood are greatly affected. The Shandong provincial government has already proposed a resolution to ban the import of foreign wheat flour, and we are requesting that the central government implement it. We feel the same way. In this time of foreign troubles and domestic worries, when the countryside is on the verge of bankruptcy and commercial transportation is in a desperate situation, if we do not impose heavy taxes on foreign rice and wheat flour and allow them to flood in, then our country will not perish from foreign troubles, but from the bankruptcy of the rural economy. The association's heart feels the danger and it is difficult to remain silent. Leaders of the Shanghai Municipal Council and the Bureau are concerned about the people's suffering and are always ahead of others. Therefore, we are submitting a special request, asking you to examine and forward it to the central government, ordering the Ministry of Finance to earnestly implement it to maintain agricultural production and alleviate the people's suffering. This would be greatly beneficial.

Shanghai Christianity Pays Attention to Moral Education, Soliciting Moral Education Novels 157

The Shanghai Christian Five-Year Movement Door 進 Association, in view of the decline of modern morality, which is largely due to the influence of lower-level reading materials, and especially of obscene novels, has organized a Moral Education Novel Solicitation Committee, and has appointed Zhao Jinqing, Zhou Zhiyu, Wang Wanbai, and three others as members. Its original opening is as follows: Young students are the future masters of the country and society. To guide them well and not sow the seeds of moral decay and loss of shame, obscene novels and bad publications have been everywhere in recent years. Uninformed young children, once they read them, will leave a lasting and harmful impression, destroying the people and damaging the youth, which is a major problem for today's society. The enemy's strength is only a material loss, but the spiritual克伐 of these future masters is a fatal wound to the country and the village. The Association, in view of this, has launched a solicitation of moral education novels, appointed members, and raised funds, hoping to obtain good reading materials that meet the needs of the Chinese people. We hope that writers at home and abroad will not spare their treasures and contribute their writings generously. We will be grateful. (Guidelines) (1) Style: Use simple text or vernacular and new punctuation to write a long novel, or a collection of short stories can also be combined into one book. The total length should be at least 50,000 words or more. (2) Subject matter: With the spirit of Christianity as the central idea, and incorporating the old morality of our country and the new civilization of Europe and America, taking the strengths and discarding the weaknesses, both solemn and humorous, using lively and fluent language to describe interesting stories, so that readers can learn the benefits of morality in their leisure time. (3) Remuneration: After the manuscripts are collected, famous figures from the church will be invited to evaluate them and reward them with cash. A special prize of 200 yuan, a first prize of 100 yuan, a second prize of 50 yuan each for two people, and a third prize of 25 yuan each for four people. Other good works will be given book coupons at our discretion. Unselected manuscripts will be returned. (4) Deadline: The deadline for submissions is the end of September of this year. Submissions from outside the city will be based on the date of the postmark. Mailing address: No. 1703 Jing'an Temple Road, Shanghai.

###济生会为乾县惨灾乞赈

中国济生会据陕西乾县振务分会报称，乾县酷遭大旱，为时五载，田野荒芜，村舍丘墟，富者早成饥民，贫者转死沟壑。迨至今春，雨泽又复愆期，丰登望绝。所余灾黎，经此奇劫，房屋衣物变卖已尽。当此青黄不接，大地赤日，求菜根而莫寻，满腹惨苦，呼苍穹而不应，水尽山穷，逃生无路。凡各村堡出亡几空，时睹街头巷尾，割爱弃子，号啼声嘶者，呼饥莫救；持刀自杀者，饿至垂危，倒卧路侧者，鹄面鸠形，待死乞怜者，讨饭无门，沿途攫食者，甚或饥饿难忍，呼号发狂者，种种惨状，笔难尽述。所望海内仁人，大开鸿慈，或施粮设立粥厂，或赐款办理急赈，救之则生，不救则死。性命呼吸，不能稍待。苍苍帝天，哀哀父母，能救一命，即一人之再生父母也。噫！惨哉！该会据报情形如此，忍泪泚笔，代为呼吁，即众人亦不堪卒读云。

招商局四码头案上诉审理 162

为李国杰染病

假沪法院审理

轮船招商局总经理李国杰，因将四码头擅自借外债，抵押与美商中国营业公司，及行贿陈孚木七十万两一案，经交通部检举，送经上海地方法院判决，李国杰处有期徒刑三年。李不服，向江苏高等法院提起上诉。惟李因患病，迄仍居上海医院内，所以高等法院，仅传证审理，而李不能到庭。故据李之声请，假上海地方法院法庭审理，业已定期于本月二十六日开庭审理，届期审判长预先来沪，组织法庭云。

小肉票脱险后忽病死 163

各绑匪昨续讯一过

无关者二人先摘释

世界银行跑街绍兴人胡鹤年，家住汇山路四百九十三号门牌，本年二月廿四号深夜一时许，突被绑票多名侵入，将胡之二岁子国安绑去，并将值洋数十元之饰物刦去。经胡报告捕房，请为查缉。嗣经总稽查处华总探长陆连奎侦悉是案绑匪匿迹处所，乃督同探长刘绍奎、冯志铭、邵景范、探目周鸿林、孙德福等分别在东西华德路六百三十五号、辣斐德路同裕里八号、霞飞路月华坊二十三号、蒲石路四百零二号，先后拘获绑匪王为生、张颂尧、孙志明、朱忠更（又名更龙）、刘钦、俞季生、钱锡红、陈孚亮（陆军四十七师参议）、妇人余小妹、吴周氏、吴玉春、马阿凤等十二名口，抄获盒子炮一支、子弹二百零六粒。并据朱忠更之供词，在宁波县属马村将肉票救出，带回上海。讵未及一日，胡国安忽满身密布红点，形同天花，由其有属延北福建路痧痘儿科专家徐丽洲医生诊治，据诊断结果，谓系湿瘰。胡家以既属湿气，当无大碍，故处之泰然。乃不料至本月六日突然毙命。昨此案由第一特院刑庭长钱鸿业开庭绩讯，捕房律师钱恂九起称，本案先拘获王为生、张颂尧、孙志明、余小妹等，经王供出须拘捕朱忠更，方知肉票下落，捕房乃设法将朱及其余一干人拘获，抄得朱忠更之图章一枚，该图章即系原告所接勒赎信未署名之图章，经朱之供词，始将肉票在宁波救出，乃未及六日遽而病死，故今日不能到庭。遂将徐医生之药方及肉票之肖影呈案，而陈孚亮、钱锡红，因无证据，故不予起诉，应请先行摘释云云。钱庭长乃谕陈孚亮、钱锡红开释。继由刘绍奎探长投禀拘捕各被告及调查情形一过，并称在朱忠更处抄获奶粉瓶一只、起首图书一个，查该奶瓶系恐肉票尚须吃奶，故而购备，至起首图书上之地点，全属伪造，缘现今租借房屋，均须具保，该图章即用以租屋时盖于保单上用者，亦即呈案。经钱庭长核禀，当向各被告逐一质讯之下，谕令分别还押，改期再讯。

上松长途汽车今日开始通车上下午来回十二次 164

松江西门外起，迤东至上海县属北桥，衔接沪闵路止，由松上两县建筑长途路线，曾经松邑绅商殷石笙，取得营业专利权，筹集巨资，创办上松长途汽车公司，向英商购置最新工车辆，与沪闵公司商洽联运。自去冬试车以来，商民莫不称便。惟该路松上两县交界建筑之汇桥工程未竣，故双方车辆，不能直达，引以为憾。现悉该桥工程，业已告竣，定于本月十五日起上松沪闵两公司，彼此直放车辆，该路全线，约四十余公里，每句钟可以到达上海总站，设在国货路沪闵长途汽车公司内，松沪总站设在松江马路桥上松汽车公司。兹探得行车时刻及联票价目，分志如下。本路班车时刻照常。上海至松江快车，上午由沪闵车站开出，第一次八时半，第二次十时半，第三次十一时半，下午第四次一时半，第五次三时半，第六次五时半。到松乘客，除土山湾站，亦可购票上车外，其余经过马桥、汇桥、华阳桥、新东门、竹竿汇、卢神庙各站，祇准乘客

乾丰泰烛号小主被人枪杀 165

经理陈乾顺受重伤

案情离奇真相未明

昨晚九时四十五分，法租界菜市路口，发生枪杀案，真相未明。兹将调查所得，纪述于下。

汉口分设支号 166

乾丰泰香烛号，开设法租界东新桥菜市路口第五十号至五十二号，已十有余年。店主为甬人陈庭椿，年四十九岁，妻陈氏，年四十二岁，膝下仅一子，名芝奎，现年二十八岁，娶二妻，均早逝，仅留一子，名毛头，年方五龄。所有店中一切事务，昔日均由陈庭椿管理，历年经营，颇有赢余。庭椿乃于前年往汉口另设丰顺，本人则在汉主持一切，所有沪号事务，另托同乡人陈乾顺为经理，其子芝奎，时常往来沪汉，专事批送货物等。

弄中枪声何来 167

三日前，芝奎因汉口缺货，乃特乘轮来沪，向沪号取货，包裹妥当，即于昨晚八时许，雇乘人力车数辆，送往停泊在虹口江华轮上寄出，于九时三十分左右，仍乘原车回店，下车后，以颇觉乏力，即直入店旁私弄内进屋登楼安息。讵芝奎方拟进门时，弄内隐处突跃出暴徒二名，各持手枪，一见芝奎，即不问情由，各向其轰击一枪。芝奎受创后，亟反身出弄奔逃，时该号经理陈乾顺正在结算帐目，忽闻隔壁弄内突起枪声，甚为惊诧，以该弄系该号私有出入要道，因何来此枪声，乃亟亟奔出店堂探视。

两人一死一伤 168

当陈乾顺奔至店门时，但见小老间芝奎，正向爱多亚路直奔，所穿灰色衬绒袍上，血渍斑斑，后面并无追赶者。陈知有意外，乃将其一把拖住，讯问根由，讵话声未绝，陈乾顺身旁枪声又起，身倒地，芝奎亦于斯时创痛加剧，踣倒于地。及附近岗捕闻警赶到，奈凶手已于人丛中逸去，乃亟报告捕房，赶派探捕到来，并用车将受伤二人，车送仁济医院，奈芝奎因受伤过重，竟当场身死，即转送辅元堂，候今晨报请法院检验。

[P捕房侦骑出>

事后调查，得悉芝奎身中二枪，均在重要部位。陈乾顺年三十九岁，身部共中三枪，左肩一枪，子弹直穿而过，臀部中一枪，子弹由右小腹而出，右大腿一枪，伤势至重，恐有性命之忧。法捕房方面对于此案，甚为注意，当晚即侦骑四出，追寻线索，至于是否仇杀，成竟另有隐情，一时未能遽断，据四邻称述，陈氏父子在沪多年，向极和蔼，当不致积有怨仇云。下车，不准上车。松江至上海快车，由上松车站开出，上午第一次七时，第二次九时，第三次十一时，下午第四次一时，第五次三时，第六次五时。到沪乘客，经过卢神庙、竹竿汇、新东门、华阳桥、汇桥、马桥各站祇准上车，不准下车，其票价单程票，每张大洋八角，松沪来回票，每张大洋一元二角，以三日为有效期间。孩童长不满三英尺半者免费，在三英尺半以上者，照章购全票。行李代运，另订规程。

并悉松江至佘山地方，风景极佳，上松公司，备有专往佘山汽油船，如乘客欲往此山游览胜景者，在沪闵车站，带购船票，每张大洋八角云。

本埠日本民团发生侵吞公款案 169

昨日日文上海日报云，本埠日本民团，突然发觉会计课长侵吞公款案件，情节颇为重大，直至十三日午後，始将关系新闻，准许登载。查此案发觉后，十日午後，日本总领事馆警察，突然大活动，长田部长将住居北四川路丁兴里百十六号上海居留民团会计课长田帘平逮捕，翌日更由佐藤部长樋口刑事搜索其住宅结果，搜获银行存折、借用证书、保险契约证书等，关系证据甚多，日来开始严重审讯，将移司法办理。当此事发觉之前，外间已有田任民团会计课肥缺，不免有侵吞公款之谣，民团团部同人闻讯，曾将关系帐簿严重查究，不料竟查出约○○元，已被侵吞，于是秘密讨论对策，议决呈报总领事馆，至十日领事馆，遂将该犯逮捕云。

法租界修租脚踏车行停业风潮昨讯 170

法公董局另订邮租车辆规则

党部传讯市商会转呈请交涉

新声社云，法租界修理出租脚踏车行四十余家，因反对法公董局征收修理特捐，被法当局停供水电，不能营业，致演成全体停业风潮。连日各同业除静候各机关各团体援助调处外，尚无其他争执事件发生。但法当局见该业停业态度坚决，且无轨外行动，亦无如何压迫行为。微闻法

六旬老妇诉奚龙生确定母子身份 171

奚本人否认老妇为生母

老妇坐庭隅竟双泪交流

—两造律师在庭上微有争执—

年将六旬之妇人黄周氏，以已故富户奚鹤铭之子奚龙生，系伊所生，昔年伊生此子时，因已有两子，且家道贫寒，无力抚养，遂将此子由李瑞林经手，抱送与人，迄将三十载。初以不知着落，前岁始悉已为奚氏收养。但伊兹既年迈，应受生子赡养，乃往交涉，讵龙生竟不承认该妇为亲生之母，故延吴经熊律师，向第二特区地方法院对龙生提起遗弃之诉，旋经人调解，由龙生给该妇巨款，订立声明书，案遂了结。现黄周氏对于前订之声明书，以签字时并不知道其内容，伊与龙生之母子关系，自不受该声明书之拘束，是以又延律师三数人，具状第一特区地方法院，对奚龙生提起确定母子身份之诉，并将奚鹤铭之妻奚黄氏列为第二被告，业经该院杨鹏推事一再开庭传审。昨晨，又届续讯之期，原被两造及双方律师五人均到案，杨推事先传讯证人李瑞林，由李将昔年以原告所生之子抱送与奚家，暨去岁原告对奚龙生起诉后和解各情，详细陈述毕，原告律师尚欲请传证人黄宝和、吴经熊等到案质证，并以第二被告迄未遵传到庭，亦请补传到案，俾令其证明收养奚龙生之经过，庭上则认所请皆非必要，双方律师旋辩论至声明书一点，原告律师张舍我谓被告律师李祖虞、秦联奎，皆系该声明书中之证人，请求制止该两律师对于声明书部份之辩护权，张律师并称，“律师系雇佣性质，祇要给他钱，是无所不为的。”李秦两律师闻此语，大不满意，谓张律师出言侮辱全体律师人格，请书记官将其所言记录，杨推事当以张所请制止辩护权一点，于法无据，随即裁决不准，并仍命双方律师依法进行辩论，而被告律师终以原告起诉，于法律则无根据，于事实又无证明，要求驳斥，原告律师则以本案系伦理问题，不能以寻常法律之时效束缚之，各持理由，互辩良久，庭上嗣向原被两造询问最后之意见，据黄周氏称，当初李瑞林抱去时，祇言系送与赵家，直至四年之前，方由李说明系在奚家，故我一知此子下落，即要求赡养，务请庭上饬令被告认我为母，俾接续香烟等语。被告奚龙生供此妇实不是我之生母，先父祗云生我者为徐氏，今此妇无非敲诈云云，此时原告黄周氏坐于庭隅，双泪交流，厥状至为可悯，杨推事以本案业已审讯终结，遂谕候四月十八日宣判。

当局又有更进一步之对付办法，兹将昨日各项消息，探录于后。

另订规则　法公董局以此次征收界内各脚踏车行修理特捐，竟遭反对，即停供拒纳捐税各车行水电，以示惩戒，但此项压迫办法，非特不能使各车行屈服，反引起全体车行之团结一致，互相援助，全体停业，闻法当局除饬探捕分赴各车行催领照会费外，因均不愿捐纳，故连日已将停供水电各车行水电表一律拆卸，一面并另订出租车辆规则，凡出租车辆，均须填具法文单据，以便查考，据该业负责人表示，此项单据，除各汽车行已实行外，脚踏行因营业细微，向无此项规定，倘一经实行，则每车行均须雇用法文书记一人，故按月开支，必须更多一成，何能负担，且脚踏车行，何能与汽车行相提并论，决难承认。查汽车行之所以有此规定者，为防止不正当行为人之租车，以便查考，而脚踏车租，向无此等不正当行为，更属不必多此一举，故各同业除一并反对外，此事断难实行。

黨部傳詢　上海特别市党部民训科、于昨日下午·传唤脚踏车行贩制同业公会代表王涤生·王接通知、即偕同各代表前往面洽、由民训科特派朱亚揆接见、详询此次法公董局征收捐照费之过情形、允为据实转咨市政府、向法当局交涉、一面复劝各代表在交涉期内、应静候解决、切勿有越轨行动、各代表均唯唯而退。

社会局批　上海市社会局，对此次法租界脚踏车行被迫停业，据该业公会详呈经过，请求交涉一案，于昨日批示云，社字第一零五一七号，具呈人贩制脚踏车业同业公会，呈一件，为转呈法租界全体车行被迫停业，吁请援助由，呈悉，已据情呈请市政府，转函法租界当局交涉矣，仰即知照，此批。

商会复函　上海市商商、于昨日特函复上海市修租脚踏车业同业公会云、迳启者、本月十三日、接展来函、以贵同业在法租界者、除缴纳巡捕捐分类营业捐外、近又新增特税、因同业异议、即断水电、以为要挟、请予交涉等情、查此事先经贩制脚踏车同业公会、函同前情、经于本月十一日、分呈市党部市社会局、请其转向法租界当局义涉取消在案、来函因系一事、无庸再转、候奉批后、另函知照可也。

商会转呈　市商会昨呈市党部及社会局云，呈为据情呈请事，案据本市贩制脚踏车业同业公会函称，属会兹据上海法租界全体脚踏车行，万急代电称，上海法租界公董局增加特捐，敝同业无力负担，困苦情形，曾于东日函请贵会迅予设法，再向法公董局据理交涉，兹本日法公董局派电灯局逼迫同业，将水电线剪断，施行压迫手段，致敝同业遭受蹂躏，停止营业，用敢代电，仰乞迅予交涉，一面再请代向党政机关并各法团援助，临电迫切，不胜待命，等语到会，据此，查属会前由法租界全体脚踏车行联名盖章，迭次来函，请向法公董局声请取消增捐，以苏商困等情，曾推派代表，面谒法公董局总辩，沥陈各车行本微利薄，营业不振，以及纳税繁重，开支浩太，种种苦衷，据情转达，函请法公董局收回成命在案，惟法公董局迄未邀准，兹据代电前情，除备文转呈上海市党部社会局代为请援助外，理应备函转呈，仰祈钧会主张公道，赐予援助，等情到会。据此，查脚踏车例有车照，若再增加特捐，在本征利薄之车商，殊属不堪负担，今竟剪断各车商水电线，为强迫抽捐计，施行实属过当，理合据情呈请仰乞钧会鉴核，傭赐迅向法当局设法交涉制止，藉维业务，实为公便。

东台同乡会紧急会议 172

东台旅沪同乡会，昨据会员费永益、王德昌投会报称，向在沪西徐家汇镇华界桥堍（在法捕房警亭西边）摆设水菓摊并捐有卫生局饮食捐、财政局摊基捐等执照，讵前日下午四时许，突有法捕房大号卡车，装载华越巡捕十余名，强将费等之水菓食物及一切器具，一并装入卡车，疾驶而去。窃费等素以小本经营，维持生活，所设之水菓摊，又属华界辖境，该法捕房竟敢越界干涉，强将物件夺去，此种举动，不独妨碍平民生计，抑且有伤我国主权，为此特行来会报告，仰即予以援助等语，该会据报，即发通告召集紧急会议，拟呈请市府，迅向法领严重抗议，并请求市党部及市商会竭力援助。

Arrest of Public Prosecution Criminal Cases by the Police During the Western Spring Holiday 173

Currently, it is the Western Spring Holiday, commonly known as the Foreign Qingming Festival. All Western officials in this city are on leave. The Public Concession's Municipal Council also ceased operations for four days starting yesterday. All public prosecution criminal cases that each police station should send to the First Special Court for trial daily have been temporarily suspended and must return to normal on Tuesday (the 18th) next week. Therefore, during these four days, excluding Sunday's regular holiday, the court will only hear civil and criminal self-accusation cases in the morning and afternoon each day.

Petition from Residents of the Southern City to Add Patrol Posts 174

Yesterday, merchants and residents in the area of the Southern City Local Court, including Xu Weiji Hat Factory, submitted a petition to the Municipal Public Security Bureau stating, "Respectfully submitted, our area, the section of the Southern City Local Court, West Hu Minnan Zhelu, and Shears Bridge Road, has seen increasing prosperity and densely populated residences in recent years. However, no additional patrol posts have been added to date, leading to robberies and injuries during the day and thefts at night, which are frequently heard of. Recently, the shooting of a patrol officer near this area this month, traced back to its cause, is due to the insufficient number of patrol posts and the lack of timely response, resulting in this unexpected disaster. It has also made travelers uneasy and residents restless. However, the residents in our area bear the same tax obligations as other citizens and should receive the same level of protection. Therefore, we especially implore your esteemed office to promptly plan and add patrol posts in our area and implement them as soon as possible to enhance protection and maintain public safety. This would be a great benefit." This is submitted to the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau by Xu Weiji Hat Factory, Sanxing Company, etc.

Proposed Method for Emergency Treatment of Schistosomiasis in Northern Jiangsu 175

National Physician Tang Liupu wrote to this newspaper, "Having read the April 12th Shanghai Great Evening News, the spring weather in northern Jiangsu is extremely dry, and schistosomiasis has been discovered, spreading throughout Huaiyin, Huaian, Lianshui, Siyang, Muyang, Suqian, and other counties. The symptoms initially involve obstruction of the lower burner and difficulty breathing in the lungs. After three days, the abdomen gradually swells up like an overturned basin, becoming as hard as iron. After this stage, the patient becomes unable to speak and dies within a week at most. Those suffering from this disease are mostly men, with women being extremely rare." According to the classics, "The lower burner is like a ditch," and "The large intestine is the organ of conduction, from which changes arise." This indicates that there is too much dampness, qi, and blood. If people are affected by the dry heat of heaven and earth, bowel movements often become blocked and unsatisfying. After prolonged accumulation, impurities will inevitably overflow into the lower burner. The lungs and large intestine are internally and externally related. If the large intestine is blocked, breathing in the lungs will naturally be difficult. Heat in the qi phase will inevitably extend to the blood phase. Heat in the blood will lead to stasis, and after extreme stasis, worms will be generated. Women have menstrual periods every month to discharge these, so this type of symptom is extremely rare. In my opinion, this disease should be carefully examined through inspection, questioning, listening, and palpation. If the patient is physically strong or even withdrawn, speaks softly but forcefully, and is usually capable of hard work, then a modified Taoren Chengqi Decoction should be used to purge, with small doses of Mangxiao, Dahuang, Gancao, Taoren, Zhishi, Gualouren, Danpi, Laimiaozi, and Guiwei being tested. If this is ineffective, a large dose of Fangfeng Tongsheng Wan can be decocted and taken, treating both the exterior and interior. Even for those with spiritual afflictions, the urgent should be treated symptomatically. After purging, Wumei, Baihe, and Gancao soup can be used to regulate. The physique of northerners is generally stronger than that of southerners. In treating disease, it is only necessary to seek appropriate remedies, without seeking lofty theories. I wonder if this is appropriate, so I am specifically submitting it to various newspapers for publication, hoping to discuss it with knowledgeable physicians from various regions."

Sudden Attack with Three Stabs 177

Xu Yonggui Suspects Wife of Being Seduced

Xue Aquan Wrongfully Stabbed

Huang Zigen, a 55-year-old man from Pudong, has been running the Jurulin Vegetarian Restaurant outside Xiaonanmen, Nancang Street. His wife, Zhu, is 56 years old. They have a son named Yinsheng, who married Lin, both of whom have passed away, leaving behind a daughter named Gendi, who is currently 16 years old. Two years ago, in the first month of the lunar year, she was betrothed to Xu Yonggui, son of Xu Shunrong, the owner of the Xutai Hing Bucket Shop on Huayi Street outside Dadongmen, through a matchmaker. Yonggui, also known as Boying, is 23 years old and originally from Chuansha. His father, Shunrong's Xutai Hing Bucket Shop, has a very prosperous business, so he has branches in Xiaonanmen and other places. Yonggui also assists with the store's business. After Gendi married into the family, they initially lived together in the old store on Huayi Street, and the relationship between husband and wife was still harmonious. However, since Gendi became dissatisfied with her father-in-law Shunrong's behavior last year, the couple moved to their old home in Jinjiaqiao, Chuansha, Pudong. Yonggui also stopped working at his store and was subsequently introduced to work at Jiang Shengtai Bucket Shop at No. 36, North Santai Lane, Laozha Bridge. At around 11:00 AM yesterday, Yonggui, carrying a sharp blade, rushed to the Jurulin Vegetarian Restaurant, grabbed his associate Xue Aquan, and asked if he was named Xue Aquan. Xue responded in the affirmative. Yonggui instantly raised his eyebrows, his face turned pale, and he shouted in a murderous tone, "Good!" He immediately raised his hand and slapped Xue in the face. Xue, after being struck, was confused and stood there dumbfounded. Yonggui then pulled out the concealed sharp blade from his side and stabbed Xue repeatedly. Xue raised his hands to resist. At that moment, the other associates in the restaurant were shocked and immediately rushed forward, holding Yonggui down and disarming him. However, Xue had already been stabbed three times, one on each arm and one in the left abdomen, about an inch wide. The internal organs were vaguely visible. If it had been any deeper, the intestines would have protruded. At the time, after Xue was wounded, blood flowed from the wounds, and he collapsed to the ground in extreme pain. Seeing this, the associates immediately reported Xu Yonggui to Xie Chuping, the guard at the 15th post, and took him to the Third Section of the First District. Meanwhile, Xue was taken to Shanghai Hospital for treatment. It is said that if there are no complications, his life will not be in danger. After the hospital doctors bandaged his wounds, he was sent to the Third Section of the First District. During the preliminary trial, Xu Yonggui confessed, "My wife, Gendi, often goes to her mother's house, which is the Jurulin Vegetarian Restaurant. I didn't mind. However, recently, Gendi's temperament has changed drastically, and after going to her mother's house, she must be urged repeatedly before she is willing to return home. I became suspicious and paid attention to her every move. Until the day before yesterday, I suddenly found a note in her jewelry box with the words 'Zhang Xingen of Deyilou in Shanghai City to be delivered to Zhang Bingnan.' I questioned Gendi repeatedly, and she claimed that Zhang Bingnan was one of the associates used by her mother's family and was introduced by Xue Aquan. As for whether or not a physical relationship had occurred, Gendi naturally refused to say so. However, I thought that Xue was seducing my wife and having affairs with others, and this note clearly showed that there must be a secret between Gendi and Bingnan. Therefore, I was greatly angered and could not contain my anger for a moment, so I carried a sharp blade and went to my wife's family today to fight Xue to the death." Xue Aquan confessed that he was 26 years old and from Wuxi. "Although Yonggui often came to the store, I never talked to him and never introduced his wife, Gendi, to Zhang Bingnan, who works in the store. So I really don't understand why Yonggui came today and stabbed me." As the testimonies of both parties differed, and the matter involved injury, a document was prepared and sent to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for interrogation at around 4:00 PM.

Two Deliverymen Suddenly Become Extravagant, Raising Suspicions 178

Investigation Reveals Embezzlement of a Considerable Amount of Funds

Each Sentenced to Three Months of Imprisonment

Zhao Zhongwei from Ningbo and Cao Xinren from Zhenjiang, deliverymen at the China Coal Briquette Company at No. 407 Caishi Street, Hongkou, became addicted to prostitution and gambling. Their income could not cover their expenses, making it impossible to cover up the embezzlement of over 700 yuan. Previously, managers Lu Hengtong and Ye Shunyu noticed the sudden change in the two men's appearance and their luxurious clothing. They thoroughly investigated the accounts handled by the two men, confirming that Zhao Zhongwei had embezzled 256.5 yuan and Cao Xinren had embezzled 459.5 yuan. They immediately reported the situation to the Hongkou Police Station, which dispatched detectives to arrest Zhao and Cao and send them to the First Special District Court for interrogation and detention. Yesterday, Judge Wu Zehan summoned Chief Prosecutor Wang Zuzhe to court for a continued trial. Zhang Tianyin, the police station's lawyer, presented the previous events, stating that the defendants had admitted to using the funds in the police station and requested the court to conclude the case as soon as possible. The two managers, Lu and Ye, testified about the events, presenting the account books and pointing out the amount embezzled by the two defendants. They also hired a lawyer to request a civil lawsuit, demanding full repayment. When questioned, the two defendants admitted guilt and begged for leniency. Judge Wu sentenced Zhao Zhongwei and Cao Xinren to three months of imprisonment each as a warning. The number of days of detention before the judgment is confirmed will be calculated at two days to one day of imprisonment. Each must return the amount claimed by the plaintiff.

Yan Zhengbao Accused of Seducing a Widow, Abandoning Her After Starting a Relationship 179

Liu Wang, a 35-year-old woman from Yangzhou residing at No. 96 Dunrang Lane, Rue Amiral Bayle, French Concession, whose husband, Hua Jianzhong, has passed away, has filed a lawsuit with the Second Special District Court, accusing Yan Zhengbao (51 years old), a fellow villager and owner of Tian Shunxing, a wooden rickshaw repair shop at No. 142 Route Hennequin, of seducing a widow and abandoning her after starting a relationship. She requests that the case be thoroughly investigated and prosecuted under Articles 344 and 363 of the Criminal Law, and she also requests incidental civil compensation for living expenses and damages. Her complaint states that after her husband's death, she relied on her own efforts to raise her son and daughter-in-law and to uphold her chastity. The defendant coveted her beauty, repeatedly teased and seduced her with sweet words and financial enticements, giving her clothing and food, causing her to fall into his trap. In the ninth month of the lunar calendar in the 20th year of the Republic (1931), she lived with the defendant and allowed him to have sexual relations with her. At that time, she brought gold and silver jewelry worth over 300 yuan and handed it over to the defendant. She also had a building at No. 13 Yufuli rented out by the defendant. The defendant gradually sold off the jewelry and spent the money. By June of last year, the defendant used trickery to have her move to Yuancheng Lane on Route Lafayette, giving her 15 yuan per month for expenses, but soon after, he abandoned her and ignored her. She requests an investigation and, incidentally, civil compensation for living expenses until she reaches 60 years old, totaling 4,500 yuan, and damages for property loss of 360 yuan. The court, based on the complaint, summoned the defendant. The defendant's lawyer, Wang Shi, presented a defense, stating that the defendant and the plaintiff are relatives by marriage, as the defendant's daughter is married to the plaintiff's son. After the relative Hua Jianzhong passed away, the plaintiff smoked opium and opened a "swallow den" to make a living. In the autumn of the 20th year of the Republic, because the plaintiff and her son were helpless, she begged Chen Yuanliang to ask the defendant for help. The defendant, considering that they were relatives, allowed the plaintiff and her son to stay at his home, and he also ordered her to quit smoking. However, the plaintiff was addicted and, after staying for more than a month, gradually returned to her old ways, secretly going out to smoke and not returning late at night. The defendant's persuasion was ineffective. By the spring of last year, the defendant urged the plaintiff to take her son back to their hometown, but she begged Chen Yuanliang to plead for her, and she and her son sought a house to live in separately. However, after moving out, she still came to borrow money from time to time. The defendant, unable to bear the annoyance, refused her. The plaintiff held a grudge and falsely accused him of seduction and fraud. He requests that witnesses be summoned and questioned to clarify the matter. The court originally scheduled the trial for yesterday afternoon. Both parties and their lawyers reported on time. However, because the presiding judge was on vacation, the hearing was postponed and re-summoned for further verification.

—Taking a Large Dose of Foul-Smelling Disinfectant, Life in Danger—

Mr. Ren, a native of Jiangyin residing at No. 67 Shoupin Lane, Ward Road, is nearly sixty years old. Chen Xiaoliu, a Victim of Economic Oppression, Commits Suicide by Drinking Hydrochloric Acid 181

Chen Xiaoliu, a 35-year-old man from Changshu, residing in the back three rooms of the living room of Tang Pan, a sub-tenant at No. 1 Zhenghua Lane (south of the railway), Datong Road, Zhabei, used to make a living selling oil bean curd vermicelli. Recently, Chen, under economic pressure, applied for a loan of 20 yuan from the Poverty Alleviation Office on Minli Road, stating that the payment would be made on April 10th. Later, Chen asked a shoe store to guarantee the loan, and the Poverty Alleviation Office sent someone to investigate the guarantor. However, the store happened to be closed for three hours for the Qingming Festival, and the family had gone to sweep the tombs. When the investigator from the Poverty Alleviation Office arrived at the store, he saw that it had closed. Therefore, on the 10th, when Chen went to collect the money, he was refused. After Chen returned home, he was depressed. Yesterday morning, at around 8:00 AM, Chen took a black soy sauce bottle, not knowing where he bought hydrochloric acid, and returned home. The people in the house did not pay attention to it. A short while later, Chen screamed in pain on the bed. After inquiring, it was learned that he had drunk hydrochloric acid. He was immediately sent to Pushan Hospital for treatment. After the doctor used medication to wash out his stomach, the poison was expelled. However, according to the doctor, some of the poison had already spread into the lungs, so he was quickly sent to Baolong Hospital in the concession for treatment. Unexpectedly, when he was sent to Baolong Hospital, Chen was already dying. The doctor, seeing the situation, immediately gave him a strong heart injection. However, the treatment was ineffective, and he died at around 10:00 AM. The body has now been sent to the Hongkou Coroner's Office for examination. The deceased has a wife and a son, Wang, who is 27 years old, and a son named Jinlong, who is three years old. There are no other family members in their hometown.

Reader's Advisory 188

A Collection of Letters Discussing the Question "Can We Return to the Countryside?" 189

(8) A Letter from Mr. Xu Xianfu from This Port: Can the Missionary-Style Education Method Save the Countryside?

To the Reporter and Mr. You Huaihao: Regarding the issue of returning to the countryside, Mr. You Huaihao, with his many years of research as a rural expert and practical experience as an agricultural practitioner, advises Mr. Xiongsheng to return to the countryside. However, this provokes a rebuttal from Mr. Liu. I do not want to discuss Mr. Liu's theory. However, regarding Mr. You's opinion (advising Mr. Xiongsheng to return to the countryside), if it is only for personal life, I think it can be said. As for using his own strength, there is a possibility of creating a new-style Peach Blossom Spring. I think there is room for discussion with Mr. You. This may be the opinion of a fool. I hope it is not considered showing off my slight skill before an expert. The state of the Chinese countryside is like this: among the 336 million farmers, 186 million are landless farmers, and 150 million are farmers with land. Among them, 50 million wealthy farmers occupy 79% of the agricultural land. This is enough to prove the differentiation of the class in Chinese rural areas. Among the landless farmers, there are tenants and hired farm hands. At the same time, we tried to investigate China's export commodities in the customs import and export trade statistics. Nineteen is the raw materials of agricultural products. It is said that Chinese rural production has largely become commodity production, that is, it has become the raw material production base of imperialism. Directly and indirectly, it is dominated by the international market. However, we should also pay attention to the fact that China is a country that has been economically invaded by imperialism. Under their economic domination, our urban capitalist industry has been developed, but it is largely in their hands. National industries, with weak capital accumulation, cannot compete with imperialism. Therefore, capitalists, merchants and usurers with a small number of currencies turned to rural investment. Among them, there is the formation of heavy-handed exploitation. At the same time, we should also pay attention to the fact that the feudal warlord system exists in China. They are in a superior position, in order to satisfy their private desires, in order to obtain their financial resources, and in order to cultivate their power, they used exorbitant taxes and levies to oppress the countryside. The direct impact is on the landlords and owner-farmers. The landlords again exploit the tenants. Self-cultivating farmers and tenants exploit the hired farmhands. Seeing that there is such a complex situation in the Chinese countryside, can it be like Mr. You's ideal? Can the missionary-style educational methods save the countryside and save the peasants, and create a new peach blossom source? I hope that Mr. You will not hesitate to teach me on this point. But I want to declare that I am not opposed to saving the countryside and returning to the countryside. It's just not that simple.

The Tragic Case at the Zhongshan Forest Farm 192

All Students Send a Telegram Seeking Aid

Students Remaining in Shanghai Express Indignation

(Hong Kong, 14th) The National Zhongshan University's All-Student Conference for Aiding the Forest Farm Tragedy telegraphs: "To the Shenbao Newspaper Office, for public review by all schools and academic and cultural organizations nationwide: Our school, unfortunately, suddenly experienced an unprecedented tragedy on the 8th of this month. Dean Zou Jiucheng, leveraging the lascivious power of the school president's relatives, indulged police chief Zou Libing to arbitrarily detain professors and brutally assault staff. The authorities, shielding evildoers and acting improperly, allowed the thugs to remain at large. All faculty and students are extremely indignant. The General Assembly has unanimously resolved to strike and seek a just resolution. We hereby announce the details of the tragedy to the nation: The forest police captain of our school, Zou Libing, is the school president's nephew. Because he concurrently served as the captain of President Wu's guard, he entrusted Zhang to act as the forest police. After Zhang assumed office, he privately dismissed five forest police officers. Professor and Forest Farm Director Hou Guo, believing the forest police were innocent, urged Zhang to reinstate them. Zhang, failing to fulfill his personal desires, reported to Zou Libing, who then gathered more than ten members of the school president's guard and went directly to the forest farm. They pointed pistols at Director Hou and forest farm staff members Huang and Lai, threatening them. They then detained Director Hou in the president's office, falsely accusing Huang and Lai of being communists and brutally assaulting them, causing serious injuries. They also used iron chains and large locks to secure them in the school police office. Dean Zou Jiucheng deliberately indulged the evildoers and fostered wickedness. Only after faculty and students signed and submitted a petition did they release the two to seek medical treatment. Later, President Zou not only failed to redress the grievances of these three but also falsely accused the students who upheld justice of being lawless, still protecting the perpetrator and refusing to bring him to justice. Since the incident, the entire school has been under the gunpoint of the president's guard, with no way to appeal. How can we not feel heartbroken? The entire student body, forced to do so, painfully agreed to strike, hoping that the authorities will realize their past mistakes, redress the grievances of the injured, seek guarantees for over four thousand faculty and students, protect the dignity of the sacred institution of learning, and seek the extension of human rights. Therefore, we painfully make this sacrifice and respectfully request that national cultural organizations uphold justice, show sympathy and provide assistance. We are earnestly looking forward to it. The National Zhongshan University's All-Student Conference for Aiding the Forest Farm Tragedy kowtows."

It is truly outrageous. We deeply hope that everyone will rise up together to remove this Qingfu (a symbol of evil), not be intimidated by threats, not be tempted by bribes, not lower one's own standing, not bend one's will, and fight to the end. Our association pledges to be your backing. In addition to reporting to the Ministry of Education for strict investigation, we send this telegram to express our condolences and wish you the best in your efforts. The Zhongda Students Remaining in Shanghai kowtows."

Regulations for the National Compilation and Translation Bureau 193

Passed by the Legislative Yuan Yesterday

(Nanjing, 14th) The original text of the Regulations for the National Compilation and Translation Bureau, passed by the Legislative Yuan on the 14th, is as follows: Article 1: The National Compilation and Translation Bureau is subordinate to the Ministry of Education and is responsible for the compilation and translation of books on various academic subjects. Article 2: The National Compilation and Translation Bureau compiles and translates the following types of books: (1) those concerning the dissemination of culture and advanced scholarship; (2) those publicly owned by specialized academic societies worldwide and possessing academic authority; (3) those with profound content and voluminous scope, which cannot be completed by private individuals in a short period; (4) books necessary for education; (5) terminology related to art. Article 3: Upon the order of the Ministry of Education, the National Compilation and Translation Bureau may review books, specimens, instruments, and other educational and academic supplies for use in schools. Article 4: The National Compilation and Translation Bureau shall have one Director, appointed through simplified procedures. Article 5: The National Compilation and Translation Bureau shall have twenty full-time compilers and fifteen translators, and may also appoint special compilers, all of whom shall be recommended by the Director to the Ministry of Education for engagement. Article 6: The National Compilation and Translation Bureau shall have two to four executive officers, responsible for books, accounting, and general affairs, appointed by the Director and reported to the Ministry of Education. Article 7: The National Compilation and Translation Bureau may employ staff as appropriate for drafting documents or handling other matters. Article 8: The detailed rules for the operation of the National Compilation and Translation Bureau shall be determined by the Ministry of Education. Article 9: Specialized works independently compiled and translated by domestic scholars, which conform to the provisions of the various clauses in Article 2, and have been approved by the National Compilation and Translation Bureau, shall be provided with remuneration by the National Compilation and Translation Bureau at its discretion. Those with significant contributions may, with the consent of the author, be printed by the National Compilation and Translation Bureau, giving royalties and bonuses. The rules for the aforementioned royalties, bonuses, and remuneration shall be determined by the Ministry of Education. Article 10: The measures for reviewing books, specimens, and instruments used by schools shall be determined by the Ministry of Education. Article 11: At the end of each fiscal year, the National Compilation and Translation Bureau shall prepare a report on the overall work situation of the year and the work plan for the next year, and submit it to the Ministry of Education. Article 12: These Regulations shall come into effect from the date of promulgation.

Meeting of the Design Committee of the General Association of Chinese Boy Scouts 194

—Day One—

Dai Jitao Speaks, Central Government Pays Attention to Scouting

Committee Members Review Proposals from Training and Organization Groups

Ministry of Education to Restrict Studying Abroad 198

—Study Subjects Will Primarily Focus on Science, Medicine, Engineering, and Agriculture—

Must Be Graduates of Domestic Technical Colleges or Higher and Pass an Examination

According to the Regulations for Study Abroad Certificates previously stipulated by our country, anyone who graduated from a secondary school in the country was qualified to apply to the Ministry of Education for a study abroad certificate and go abroad to study at their own expense. Later, because middle schools were divided into junior and senior levels, the current Regulations for Study Abroad Certificates stipulate that senior high school graduates have the right to obtain a study abroad certificate. The Ministry of Education has recently seen that many self-funded students spend huge sums of money to study abroad and only learn some superficial common knowledge from foreign countries. After returning to the country, they are of no benefit to the social economy, which is contrary to the original purpose of studying abroad. If this continues, it will seriously affect the economic capacity of the people. Therefore, there has long been a proposal to revise the Regulations for Study Abroad Certificates. Yesterday (the 13th) afternoon, the Ministry of Education held a ministry affairs meeting, which was attended by all section chiefs and above. It was heard that the main points for revising the Regulations for Study Abroad Certificates have been decided as follows: (1) Study subjects will primarily focus on science, medicine, engineering, and agriculture; (2) Must graduate from a domestic technical college or higher and serve for three years before being able to take the examination for government-funded students; (3) Self-funded students must graduate from a domestic technical college or higher and pass an examination before being issued a study abroad certificate; (4) For the convenience of self-funded students taking the examination, self-funded study abroad examinations will be held in major cities every year, and similar examinations may also be held in inland provinces and cities; (5) Government-funded students who pass the examination in each province and city must pass a re-examination by the Ministry of Education before being issued a government-funded study abroad certificate. Although the above points have been decided, they still need to be revised in detail in terms of the regulations at the ministry affairs meeting on the 14th before being officially announced on a set date.

The 400+ Li Long-Distance Shanghai-Hangzhou Race Is Underway 207

Bravely Set Off in the Rain Yesterday Morning

Chen Xuzhou Arrived in Minhang First

The unprecedented feat organized by the Baihong Athletics Team, the 216-kilometer long-distance Shanghai-Hangzhou race, started yesterday morning after a heavy rain under the Ying Shi Memorial Tower in Old West Gate. There were originally eighteen participants, but Zhou Wangqian was absent due to temporary foot swelling, and Kuang Shihuai withdrew halfway through the Shanghai-Minhang section. Therefore, only seventeen people started, and one less will be able to complete the first day. Minhang was halfway through yesterday's first day's journey, totaling more than 29,000 meters. Chen Xuzhou was the first to reach the Min Du Wharf. The second was Jin Zhongkang, and the time was calculated to be two hours and twenty minutes. After crossing the river, they still had to advance to Caojing. The first day ended there. The results obtained yesterday were limited to Minhang. The reporters were limited by time and could only follow and report this section. It is estimated that they will arrive in Caojing around 3:00 PM.

The night before last was a torrential downpour, and the weather was not favorable. The rain only stopped a few minutes before the race. The spirit of struggle was not slightly diminished due to the weather. What was difficult was the slippery road, and with Shen Siliang's command, they mobilized together and began to advance on the long journey of more than 400 li.

The Movement of Loudspeakers 219

— VT

Many people have a regret: that their radios do not produce a loud enough sound to use a loudspeaker. The question of how to use a loudspeaker is a common problem. The common-sense answer to this problem is that a loudspeaker needs adequate power to operate. This is like needing a lot of force to move a large stone; if a weak child tries to move a heavy stone, they will inevitably fail. Naturally, the operating power of a loudspeaker also has certain requirements.

The loudspeakers currently in use are of two types: electromagnetic (Magnetic Speaker) and electrodynamic (Dynamic Speaker). Electromagnetic speakers are further divided into horn-shaped (Horn) and cone-shaped (Cone) types. Horn loudspeakers require approximately 5-50mw of power, while electrodynamic loudspeakers require 250-1250mw. To provide this ample power, an appropriate vacuum tube must be selected for the final stage of amplification. Furthermore, to obtain this necessary power, appropriate low-frequency amplification is also necessary.

For a load power of 700mw and a load resistance of 4000 ohms, since the maximum undistorted voltage obtainable from a typical grid-leak detection method is only 0.3 volts, the required voltage amplification factor for low-frequency amplification can be calculated as follows:

P = 700mw

R = 4000

El = PR = 700 x 4000

= 53V

El is the required voltage across the load. However, in practice, the output is greatest when the load resistance is twice the internal resistance of the vacuum tube. Therefore, the total resistance, i.e., the sum of the load resistance and the internal resistance of the vacuum tube, is R + R = 2 = 3-2R. Therefore, the total voltage required for the vacuum tube plate circuit is:

E = 53V x 3-2 = 79V

However, the maximum input voltage for grid-leak detection is 0.3, so the required amplification factor is:

A = 79 - 0.3 = 260

This means that for the maximum output of grid-leak detection, an amplification factor of around 300 is needed for the loudspeaker to operate fully. However, the voltage in the grid circuit is usually not high, and to avoid sound distortion, the input power to the grid is often restricted, resulting in an amplification factor of over one thousand.

Troubleshooting and Repairing Radios (3) 220

— AA

3. Sound volume fluctuates or cuts in and out intermittently.

This problem is even more annoying than the previous two. It would be better not to hear anything at all. With faint sound, you can at least hear something. But with this problem, the sound is suddenly very loud and clear, then suddenly very faint and muffled, or completely silent. It's extremely frustrating.

The causes and solutions for this problem are listed in the table below:

Phenomenon Cause Solution

Periodic weakening of sound (Fading) Inevitable for non-high-end radios

Sound changes constantly Poor antenna installation Carefully inspect and repair

Sound cuts in and out intermittently Faulty grid leak Replace with a good one

Next time, we will discuss troubleshooting and repairing static noise.

Simple Method for Measuring Resistance 221

— Xiang

When problems occur with AC radios, simply measuring the resistance of each circuit to see if the values are accurate can quickly identify the source of the problem.

This is the latest method for testing radios in Europe and America, so it is clear that measuring resistance is a very important task. Ordinary resistance measurement requires a multimeter, but multimeters are very expensive, making it difficult for many radio enthusiasts to acquire one. Therefore, the method introduced in this article uses parts commonly available to radio hobbyists: headphones, batteries, resistors, and potentiometers. First, divide the potentiometer into equal divisions, then connect the components as shown in the diagram below. H is the headphone, P is the potentiometer, B is the battery, R is the standard resistor (value is known), and X is the resistance to be measured. After connecting the circuit, briefly connect and disconnect the headphone circuit at point K. When the circuit is briefly connected and disconnected at K, a "click" sound will be heard in the headphones. Then, turn the potentiometer knob until no sound is heard in the headphones when K is connected and disconnected. At this point, the value of R1 is the reading from point O to point A, and the value of R2 is the reading from point O to point D. Using the formula, X can be easily calculated.

Example: If R is known to be 1000 ohms, and no sound is heard in the headphones when R1 is 10 and R2 is 90, then X equals 9000 ohms.

To understand the principle behind this method, simply review the principle of the Wheatstone bridge.

(Figure 5: Introducing Line Insulator)

Various Types of Antennas (Continued) 222

— Jin Yunqiao

(2) Loop Antenna: Loop antennas are extremely easy to install and provide good results (as shown in Figure 5). A regular antenna wire about 50 meters long can be used, wound into a loop with a diameter of half a foot. Insulators should separate the two ends, and a rope should be threaded through the middle, as shown by the dotted line in the diagram. Hang it indoors, connect the lead-in wire, and you can receive radio broadcasts. When not in use, it can be taken down and folded, making it very convenient.

In addition, single-wire and multi-wire antennas for outdoor use can also be moved indoors. Iron bed frames can sometimes be used to receive radio broadcasts. For example, a 20-meter-long No. 18 insulated wire can be stretched tightly around the perimeter of a room, one foot away from the walls, yielding good results. In general, while indoor antennas are easier to install than outdoor antennas, they will not produce satisfactory results unless the radio has a sufficient high-frequency amplification stage. Therefore, a simple antenna requires a complex radio. Single-tube radios can use indoor antennas if they are very close to the broadcasting station.

Other Points to Note

The higher the antenna, the better for crystal radios and single-tube radios. However, the higher the antenna, the more static electricity it will pick up from the atmosphere. This is not noticeable for small radios, but if you use a radio with powerful high-frequency amplification, the static electricity will be amplified along with the signal, resulting in a lot of noise. In this case, indoor antennas may produce a clearer sound. Furthermore, sensitive radios can receive radio broadcasts even without an antenna or ground wire. However, they may not be able to receive distant stations as well. Do not sacrifice performance for unnecessary convenience; ensure your radio can perform to its full potential.

The direction of the antenna lead-in wire connection should ideally face the broadcasting station. For example, to receive broadcasts from Hangzhou in Shanghai, connect to the southern end of the antenna; to receive broadcasts from Beijing and Tianjin, connect to the northern end. Therefore, if you find that your radio should be able to receive a particular station but is not performing as expected, try switching the antenna lead-in wire connection.

In the first article of the previous issue, "About Power Supplies," C1C2 in the illustration was mistakenly written as C12. C2 is the capacitor in the middle of the annotation. Also, there were errors in the filtering section of the second diagram in the second article during the drafting and plate-making process. The connection method can be corrected according to the right side of the first article's illustration.

Common Sense

(6) Electrical Quantity

As mentioned above, current and voltage are directly proportional, and resistance is inversely proportional. However, we must also pay attention to one thing: electrical quantity. If we have a wooden bucket that can hold one hundred gallons of water, and it flows out at a rate of one gallon per minute, then the water will flow for one hundred minutes until it is empty. But if the bucket holds less than one gallon of water, then we will definitely not be able to get one gallon of water flowing. The principle is very clear. Therefore, when talking about current, we must first understand electrical quantity. If the source of electricity is very small, then even if we increase the voltage and reduce the resistance, we will not be able to obtain a strong current. When we say a current of one ampere, we mean that one unit of electrical quantity can pass through any part of the conductor every second. This unit of electrical quantity is called the coulomb (see Units of Electricity), which is 6.29 x 10^18 electrons or the number of charges. If a current of one ampere flows continuously for one hour, then the total electrical quantity is called the ampere-hour, which is 3,600 coulombs.

(7) Electricity

Water flows from a high place to a low place, and its force can be used to do various kinds of work (such as turning wheels). The magnitude of the water force depends on the water pressure and the amount of water flow. The same is true for electric current. When electric current flows, it can be used to light lamps, drive vehicles, and perform other kinds of work. This electrical power is also called electrical power, and it also depends on the voltage and current. The unit of electrical power is the watt. Its relationship with voltage and current is as follows: Electrical power is often represented by the letter P.

Electrical Power (Watts) = Voltage (Volts) x Current (Amperes) i.e., P = E x I

But since E = IR, P = E x I = I^2R

The capacity of a vacuum tube is also expressed as the product of the plate voltage and the plate current. For example, UX203A has a plate voltage of 1000 volts and a plate current of 125 MA, so its power is 1000 x 0.125 = 125 watts. But this is the power we input (Input). After using it to generate oscillating current, because there are many losses, the output (Output) power is at most only 50 watts. Therefore, 203A is a 50-watt vacuum tube.

The power of radio stations is also expressed in watts. The power of the central broadcasting station is 75 kilowatts (Kilowatt), which is 75,000 watts. The power of each radio station in Shanghai is mostly below 500 watts.

Free Talk

On the Bell-Ringing Youths 226

— Yu Dafu

To scold people straightforwardly and frankly, one must be a person with special privileges. In the past, there were bell-ringing elders, specially appointed by imperial grace, who wore yellow robes and carried boards, strolling idly in rural villages or market towns every day. As long as they encountered disobedient local children, they could rely on the Emperor's power to beat and scold you at will, or even drag you to the nearest yamen to sentence you to death. Now that the dynasty has changed, a new batch of bell-ringing youths specially appointed by imperial grace have been born in response to the times. They have picked up their pens and started to play this game.

Bell-ringing youths are naturally much stronger than bell-ringing elders. The elders wore those yellow linen coats with the four words "Specially Appointed by Imperial Grace" written on them, but the youths certainly disdain to wear them. Maybe they would even wear a set of modern western clothes like rebellious children. This way, firstly, they can avoid the suspicion of being loyal dogs to the master, and pretend to be upright heroes like Wu Song. They can fart in the imperial palace and urinate on people's heads. But if rebellious children of the village pinch their noses when they see them, they will forget their own stench and loudly scold you for being sneaky, downright vulgar, and daring not to show your nose to compare with them.

They can also stand in the position of a third party, hinting to the master how to deal with rebels, saying, "So-and-so, so-and-so, wasn't he done like that? Why don't you follow in his footsteps?" They will even borrow the signboard of uprightness and openly report the news, saying: "So-and-so is an alias of So-and-so, living in such-and-such place." I remember there is a section in the Zuo Zhuan called "Jian Shu Cries for the General." Duke Mu of Qin did not listen to Jian Shu's advice and sent troops. Because Jian Shu's son was also in the team, he cried and sent him off, saying: "The Jin people will meet the army at Xiao, and there are two mausoleums there. The southern mausoleum is the tomb of Xiahou Emperor, and the northern mausoleum is where King Wen avoided the wind and rain. You will surely die in this place, and I will collect your bones there." At that time, the teacher who taught us this passage said: "Jian Shu is really powerful. In his crying, he told his son the geography and strategy. This article is really written so euphemistically!" I think that modern bell-ringing youths all have the skills of Jian Shu.

Rudin in China 227

— Fu Yiye

Mr. Rudin, whom Turgenev used to represent the Russian youth of the 1840s, we must encounter many of them in today's Chinese society! For example, in a magnificent Salon or dining room, cafe, or any elegant gathering, there must be a group of young people who are good at talking, full of wisdom and enthusiasm. There, they freely express their opinions in a heated and exaggerated manner. Their excited, flushed eyes look at people like two small fireballs, and their smiling mouths constantly vibrate, opening and making loud noises, winning the sympathy and praise of those present. Sometimes, they stand up straight, raising their fists, like soldiers who are about to charge to the front line, bravely and resolutely carrying out their great ideals with the spirit of Puritan sacrifice, and passionately mobilizing the surrounding audience. Their heroic spirit is so worthy of love and respect! They observe society very clearly, they know how to destroy and how to build, they are rich in scientific and philosophical knowledge, and they also love painting, music, and literature. They will tell you how unique Goethe and Shakespeare's styles are, and how wonderful Dante's Divine Comedy is. If they accidentally walk to the piano, they will also play a section of Beethoven's famous music... In short, they are young people with multifaceted talents and full of enthusiasm. Their demeanor, clothing, voice, and smile have moved the hearts of many young people. Lively and delicate girls and young and affectionate young women are all passionately loving them, always wanting to get close to them, be led by them, and realize those lofty and far-reaching ideals...

Who knows, when these young people we admire return to their rooms in the middle of the night, intoxicated by incense, they suddenly become different people!

They think about how lovely the girl they approached during the day was; they think about how to seduce her, pull her into their arms, they know how to enjoy themselves. "Love is art." "Life without love is not worth living." These are some of the words that he is later quite qualified to say at some tea parties or seminars with an arrogant expression. Finally, he calculates how to make money, how to invite celebrities to dinner, such as vice ministers or even ministers and deans, and collude to form some societies, talk about love and beauty, publish some nonsensical and cheesy words, and praise each other to become famous. He hates that his name is not immediately as Goethe's flying around the world... After putting a half-burnt cigar into the spittoon, he falls asleep on the bed. No one knows what wonderful dreams he is pursuing at this time, but the grand words and high theories he passionately expressed during the day have long been forgotten.

Saying that he forgot may not be correct. Look, the next day he is still in a crowded place, his face flushed, his mouth grinning, wildly waving his fists, and tirelessly, excitedly and generously talking nonsense, isn't he?

Ah! Mr. Rudin of nineteenth-century Russia, when did he take the train from Siberia to China!

Go to Shanghai 228

— Zhang Mingchun

One autumn afternoon, Wang Erchi stood in front of his door, and suddenly had the idea of going to Shanghai.

He stood in front of the door, as if gazing at something, as if indulging in something.

Although it wasn't raining, the sky was always gloomy, the west wind was blowing bleakly, a few crows were cawing, looking south, Wang Er saw a panoramic view of Luo Village, saw the white belly of a stagnant water embracing the village, like a dead snake lying there, he also saw the small bridge on the river, the bridge piers were already crooked, the railings were also scattered, and the dilapidated earthen walls of the village, all of which were abandoned thatched houses of people who had left their tenants to go to Jiangnan. Further away, apart from a few landlord's blue-tiled houses, there were only some tall and short chimneys, silently facing the sky, without any smoke.

He was very strange, the village had not suffered a ruthless fire, nor had it suffered a cruel war, why would it be so desolate and frightening, the sound of the ding-dong gong of the snack seller a few years ago could not be heard, the melodious tin whistle sound that tempted the children was gone, today, he only heard a monotonous, hoarse, crow cawing annoyingly on the bare branches, in the small lanes and big lanes, only the autumn wind carried dust and fallen leaves running, a few mangy dogs, thin and bony, slept in the corners of the thatched houses, the children in the village were also as thin as the dogs, in short, the scene was full of desolation.

He stood in front of the door, as if gazing at something, as if indulging in something.

The hazy night was gradually approaching, the air was full of bats coming and going, the stubborn Wang Er, who was in his thirties, had never understood what was called melancholy, and today, countless sour tears welled up in his desolate heart unconsciously.

He thought of his more than twenty years of tenant farmer life, year after year, in frugality, endurance, hunger, and hardship, he fell into poverty inextricably. Who would want to leave their hometown, but the hometown has become a fasting prison; go to Shanghai, but how many people who have been there have had a good time?

Rambling Notes from the Thatched Cottage 229

— Zizhan

(18) Tang Caichang's Party Membership

Before discussing Tang Caichang's party membership, we must know that the party membership of Huang Ai and Pang Renquan is still in dispute. In fact, Huang and Pang were engaged in the labor movement, only knowing to serve the workers, only knowing that there was the Hunan Labor Association, and there was no so-called party affiliation. Simply because Huang and Pang were the first people to sacrifice for the Chinese labor liberation movement, all factions competed to be their ancestral tablets, and the party membership of these two people became a problem. Just as Tang Caichang was the first among the late Qing patriots to raise troops to overthrow the Manchus and die, both the Reform Party and the Revolutionary Party wanted to privately claim him as a light of their party. Zhang Taiyan briefly stated in his article "The Morality of Revolution" that in the Reform movement of the Gengzi year, Kang Youwei said that the matter belonged to Tang Caichang. Caichang was not accustomed to foreign affairs, and Long Zehou, a disciple of Youwei, showed him the way. Later, Caichang's power became increasingly strong, and he did not let Zehou know about anything. He also frequented prostitutes and banquets. Zehou became angry and fought for it but could not get it. Then, he led Wen Tingshi to Wuhan to reveal his affairs. After Caichang died, his military supplies were in Shanghai, and his colleagues stole them and fled. Therefore, the change of the Gengzi year was caused by the immorality of the Gengzi party members. Not long after, at the New Year celebration of the Minbao, a Mr. Liu came out to speak, defending Tang Caichang. He briefly stated that Caichang's uprising relied on secret societies, and the purpose of the secret societies was "to destroy the Manchus." This one sentence was enough to prove that Tang Caichang was not a member of the Reform Party. Those who communicated with Kang and Liang did so for a reason. At that time, revolutionary patriots often mistakenly regarded Kang and Liang as comrades, and Tang Caichang was not the only one. After Caichang died, Kang and Liang used him to gain a reputation for serving the king and to fool party members. His flesh was not worth eating, and his words were not worth arguing. However, Mr. Zhang Taiyan was a leader in academia and a pioneer of the revolution, and his words were respected by the people of the country, and he also said this, so Tang Caichang died with injustice. Later, Zhang Taiyan wrote a portrait of Tang Caichang, and he regretted that his revolution had not succeeded. The praise said: "The dreamy heaven, the vast Emperor, abandoned my divine state, and favored the Hu descendants. The yellow crane cries at night, annihilating this bright beauty. The head of Wenchang, the red eyes still see. (Self-note, Caichang was beheaded at Wenchang Gate after his death. It is also said that Caichang's eyes were red.) See me unharmed, write this phantom." At this time, Mr. Zhang had regarded Tang Caichang as a revolutionary comrade, and no longer belittled him as a member of the Reform Party.

The Crossroads of the Times and Love 230

— Zhang Ziping

"Scold me for being cowardly, and I cannot defend myself. But what if I weren't cowardly? Why make such a pointless sacrifice!"

But afterwards, he thought again, if everyone were like him, would the Chinese nation never have a day of liberation? Thinking also of those comrades who had been arrested, he felt infinite sadness, and almost burst into tears.

When Haiquan felt this huge contradiction, he experienced a truly indescribable mental anguish.

When he returned to Cao Shiguang's house, it was dusk. He stepped onto the stairs, unable to hear a sound. He looked up and saw only the dimness of the entire building. He went up, pushed open Qiuying's door, and saw that Qiuying was still lying sprawled on the bed as usual, breastfeeding the child.

As soon as Haiquan saw her, he felt as if he had found solace, forgetting all about the events of this afternoon, and his head stopped aching. He boldly walked to the side of the bed and sat down on the edge of the bed.

"Has Lao Cao not come back?"

"He hasn't come back all day."

Her spirit seemed very anxious, displaying an impatient expression.

"Why don't you turn on the light?"

"The switch is broken."

"Then ask the landlord on the second floor to fix it."

"Shameless! He wouldn't care about us upstairs!"

Spring and Autumn

Tobacco 231

— Zhan Lu

The saying of the ancients, "In matters of taste, mouths have the same preferences," only referred to food and drink; since the advent of tobacco, besides food and drink, we must add smoking.

In the seventeenth century, tobacco was introduced from Luzon to Fujian Province during the reign of Emperor Chongzhen of the Ming Dynasty. Soldiers on the frontier suffered from cold ailments, which could not be cured without it. However, it was very expensive; it was said that one catty of tobacco could be exchanged for a horse, and those who transported tobacco out of the pass could lead horses into the pass. Therefore, the cultivation of tobacco gradually flourished. In the mid-Chongzhen period, an order was issued prohibiting the cultivation of tobacco, with violators subject to penal servitude; however, the profits were high and the penalties were light, so how could the harm of tobacco be eradicated? Later, the penalty was increased to death; but after the strict prohibition, soldiers suffering from cold ailments often went untreated. Helplessly, they had to lift the ban and allow the people to plant it. By the end of Chongzhen's reign, even three-foot-tall children were smoking, which was the earliest era of widespread smoking in China. 丨丨 "Note 1"

As for the popularity of cigarettes in China, it has only been about thirty years. It is said that foreigners invented cigarettes in 1832 through Egyptian soldiers. At that time, a large group of camels carrying tobacco was passing through Africa and was intercepted by soldiers. They did not have pipes at the time, so they devised a method of rolling up paper strips and smoking it. Later, everyone followed suit, and the popularity of cigarettes spread throughout the world.

Famous people in the world who enjoyed smoking cigarettes include Napoleon, Bismarck, and King Edward VII of England. There are countless famous Chinese people who enjoy smoking tobacco today. During the reign of Emperor Kangxi of the Qing Dynasty, Han, the top scholar from Suzhou, always had a wine cup and a tobacco pipe in his hand. Wang Yuyang, referring to the two items of wine and tobacco, used a sentence from the Analects to ask: "If you must part with one, which of the two should come first?" Han Gong pondered for a moment and said: "Wine." It can be seen that he loved tobacco more than wine. 丨丨 "Note 2"

The only thing I want to do after a meal is to smoke urgently, as people commonly say: "A pipe of tobacco after a meal is better than being a living god." When I was smoking cigarettes, I would put down my rice bowl and want to become a living god, and if I was even a little late, it felt as if my tongue was growing hair. Since I quit cigarettes due to illness, at first, it seemed inconvenient; but now it has been five years, and after putting down my rice bowl, I absolutely do not think about smoking, which is called: "Not smoking after a meal is also being a living god."

Note 1 丨丨 Based on Pillow Worm's Trivial Sayings

Note 2 丨丨 Based on Sharing Leisurely Words

Dedicated to the Warriors 232

— Xia Tianwu

The salute dedicated to the warriors is the only true affection in the world.

The spirits of children are worn away in playthings, the spirits of women are worn away in adornments, the spirits of officials are worn away in flattery, and the spirits of merchants are worn away in abacuses and money. Only the spirits of warriors are sacrificed to the public, worn away in the trenches of gunfire and bullets.

The only stimulant for warriors is the rumbling of cannons.

Japanese people can kill Chinese people because we can also kill them. Chinese people must not kill Chinese people. The killer is Chinese, and the killed is also Chinese.

A mother's compassionate heart is concerned about the news of the warriors.

Ah! Only a few drops of red blood are left on the battlefield!

This is the greatest tragedy in the world!

The only true tears in the world are those that flow from the eyes of heroic warriors, mourning that great things cannot be done.

Those who are known in the world are not heroes; heroes all sleep in the desolate graves of unnamed warriors.

Night 233

— Xu Xiaoting

Night is dark, it is dull, it is a space rich in anesthesia. In this space that is spurned by people, the cells it organizes have no living force at all. The cold and lonely phenomenon is the same as a dead soul, yet it has no awareness or spirituality to speak of!

But the prosperous city is not like this. The modern young men and women generally prefer to pick up this spurned space, wearing away their will and anesthetizing their spirits.

The brightly lit cafes, the dance halls where men and women embrace, and the bustling streets, the meat markets, these places are built from the cold cellar of night into a layer of hot and luminous illusory realms! Fly-like humans, propping up their dazed heads, unconsciously, like flies drawn to the stench, compete in those places. At this time, they are indeed like moths that like to stir in the bright atmosphere. The night of the city is a sharp weapon for anesthetizing people's spirits. Its temporary illusion cannot exist forever. After a certain period of time, it is still cold, dark, and there is not a bit of light to be found.

Chinese people are accustomed to living the life of the night, accustomed to anesthetizing their own spirits. Night is their only pastime. But since September 18th and January 28th, the violent Japanese have come to our country and fired several awakening cannons. The countrymen who were indulging in the atmosphere of night have gradually awakened to this day.

Indeed, the light built on the cold cellar of night is temporary, it is illusory, it is too narrow to hold many people. We who are immersed in its embrace will never find true light. We must save the fresh and active vigor, and we must jump over the environmental of the night in order to reach the open road of true light!

West Lake Changes Color 234

— Xia Ying

Spring leaps at the tips of the willow branches. My heart is also pulled by something unknown. I ran to the West Lake with a heart full of sorrow. Seeing that everyone else was so happy. This time last year, the Shanghai war was raging, and there were often solar airplanes soaring over the West Lake, but this year the front line is far away from us.

The lakeside hotels were all full, and I managed to stay in a friend's room. The sound of "stockings" landing on the corridor outside the door pierced deep into my sorrowful heart!

The seven-day spring holiday passed in the blink of an eye. What did I get? Look!

On the first day, a black and white checkered scarf was wrapped around the neck.

On the second day, slender white hands held stockings. On the third day, men's suit pants were revealed under a long cheongsam. On the fourth day, fluffy hair, rosy cheeks, a floral tie, and a beige men's suit. On the fifth day, a long cheongsam, a short suit jacket, a wide-brimmed soft straw hat used by farmers in the fields, and a string of Buddhist beads hanging on the front of the garment. On the sixth day, a bicycle knocked down a child on the road, and sweat dripped down. What about the seventh day? Riding a horse and galloping on the lakeside. Gone, everything is gone.

Intoxicated in the embrace of the god of spring! The West Lake changes color. The rivers and mountains also change color!

Hotel 235

— Yan Chonglou

Metropolises are filled with travelers, so metropolises are also filled with hotels (?)

In Shanghai, the large hotels along Xizang Road and Nanjing Road meander as spectacularly as the Great Wall. Whenever dusk falls, many people head towards that Great Wall.

Hotels seem to be set up for travelers in name, but in fact, travelers who stay in hotels account for the fewest. The reason is that some travelers, considering the high cost of hotels, would rather stay overnight at their relatives' or friends' homes, while the idle young masters of the local general class leave their own luxurious houses and go to hotels to open rooms. It is said that hotels are not only fully equipped and well-serviced, but also unconstrained and free to move around! (The so-called free activities, of course, include smoking, drinking, whoring, and gambling.)

Every Saturday night, or on holidays, hotels are usually declared full. If a new hotel opens, the crowding of patrons is beyond description!

I think: "The flourishing of the hotel business is one of the reasons for the bankruptcy of the countryside."
