Shanghai Night Talk 237

— Zhang Ruogu

Polish Composers

This week, two musicians came to Shanghai. One is Frjmel, the composer of the operetta "Rose Marie"; the other is Tansmano, a modern young Polish composer.

The poet Shao Xunmei invited me to Summer Pike to watch Ms. Aluncion Granados perform Spanish dance one night. During the break, I saw an old man with a not very tall stature, a big nose, and a wrinkled face, wearing a snow-white vest and a straight black evening dress. The poet Shao told me that it was Frjmel. This time, he was traveling through Shanghai to collect information about Chinese folk music.

A few days later, the poet Shao called me, saying that he was hosting a Polish musician at the Xinghualou and wanted me to accompany him. When I arrived at the banquet, the poet Shao enthusiastically introduced me to shake hands with the young composer Tansmano, and we casually said a few words. I asked about the recent situation of the former Polish Prime Minister and world-renowned pianist Paderewski, and learned that the Polish senior musician had been on a musical performance tour in the Americas since leaving his political career.

Tansmano has a considerable position in the modern Polish music scene. Although he is not as well-known as Paderewski in the world of music, I have not heard his works, so I dare not make reckless criticisms.

This time he came to Shanghai, he felt the loneliness of an artist, because he was very popular in the music scene of Japan. He stayed in Shanghai for several days, unexpectedly received a cold reception, especially the conductor of the Shanghai Municipal Council Orchestra, Meiboqi, who was in charge of the music scene in Shanghai, did not express anything to him, and he seemed to be a little embarrassed.

From Tansmano's conversation, we can know his musical tendencies, sometimes dreaming of Ravel, sometimes dreaming of Stravinskyo

Ravel is a famous modern French composer. His style is very much influenced by his compatriot Debussy. Some people say that he is the successor of the French Impressionist musicians. His works are rich in pure musical colors.

Stravinsky is a unique writer in the modern Russian opera world. His works are completely innovative and full of oriental colors. He often likes to boldly use dissonant harmonies in his music and can achieve great success. He has a famous song called "Volga Boatmen's Song" (that is, the boatmen's song in the film "Party Soul"), which has a melancholy and sad flavor.

Tansmano has a special musical intuition, which is slightly different from the traditional Polish music tradition. The Polish music tradition can be represented by Chopin, the giant of the 19th century romantic music.

Chopin is a pianist and poet, and can also be called the soul of the piano. His style is completely lyrical, full of poetic interest, and he is a female composer and pianist. Tansmano's compositions are entirely based on national music, and he does not often rely on folk songs, but he will rediscover the essence of folk music, and his representative is called "Polish Music Score."

On this night, the poet Shao accompanied Tansmano to World College on Fooking Road to visit the ancient music performance of the Datong Music Society. Among those present were Li Shizeng, Xie Shoukang, and the female poet Fang Weide. In a music hall that could accommodate about 100 people, there were only a few dozen people listening to the Chinese ancient chamber music concert.

On the stage, the first was a solo guqin performance, High Mountains and Flowing Water, the sound of the qin was so light that it was almost inaudible. Then came a pipa solo, Wild Geese Descending on the Sandbank, and finally it seemed to be a song Bright Moon over the River, after the performance, I asked Tansmano for his thoughts on the concert.

He said: "This is the first time I've heard Chinese music, and it seems even more modern than jazz."

When I told him that it was the last remaining ancient music in China, he looked a little surprised, and at the same time, a seemingly disbelieving expression appeared on his face.

Commercial News 238

Financial Market During the Bank Holiday Was Exceptionally Desolate 239

Yesterday, the Western banks were closed for the holiday, and the situation on the market was quiet. The trading in the field was particularly calm. Cash Export Permit Issued for the First Time

New York, April 13 (Electric). Today, spot silver rose to 625, and forward silver also seemed to rise. The transaction was 4,775,000 ounces. The market situation was due to the Washington Conference and the revival of the theory of commodity inflation, so speculators made strong purchases, which led to this high price.

The Ministry of Finance received a report from Huan Street that it had issued a cash export permit to a New York general bank for the purpose of Dutch exchange. The cash will be loaded onto the Sdan Teng ship tomorrow, but the amount is unknown. This is the first cash export for exchange purposes since the gold export ban last month.

Pickled Mustard Tuber is About to be Available 259

Pickled mustard tuber is a famous product of Sichuan and is produced in large quantities. It has a wide range of uses and can be added to both meat and vegetarian dishes. It is sold in markets all year round. The new crop can be harvested a few days before Grain Rain, and it can be sold in various regions by the end of April. Here is a brief overview:

Pickled mustard tuber is made from the stems of the vegetable "mustard greens." It has a slightly salty and fresh taste. To preserve it for a long time and to facilitate long-distance transportation, it is often mixed with chili powder, which gives it a spicy taste. However, it still retains its fresh taste, and its color becomes bright red, making it visually appealing. It is packaged in ceramic jars, sealed tightly, and placed in bamboo baskets. Each jar has a net weight of 40-50 catties. The varieties and grades are as follows: (1) Lozicai from Yubei (Ba County) is the highest quality. It has a bright yellow color, and the pieces are of moderate and uniform size. It is fleshy and round, with a fresh and slightly spicy taste that does not change over time. (2) Fulingcai from Fuling is the next best. The pieces are of uneven size and may have some skin fragments. The color is also uneven, and the flesh is thinner, with a spicy and slightly fresh taste. With proper storage, it can remain unchanged. (3) Fengducai from Fengdu has a bright color and fleshy flesh, but the taste is inferior and it does not last long. It usually changes within one or two months, with the color turning from yellow to wilted and the taste becoming sour, losing all its advantages. Cunning merchants add a lot of chili powder to make it very spicy, masking the true taste. Therefore, the identification of pickled mustard tuber lies in its bright yellow color, round and fleshy pieces, and fresh and slightly spicy taste. This is the highest quality. Lacking one or two of these qualities indicates an inferior product.

Commentary

General Tang Honored as Army Commander 264

— Tianfang

Although China has a population as numerous as "carp crossing the river," the talent pool is always limited to a few individuals. A review of the political history of the past 20 years of the Republic of China reveals that the same 18 Arhats repeatedly take office, step down, and then take office again, creating a seemingly lively but ultimately unchanged situation. Is "talent scarcity" not the case?

Because of the scarcity of talent, there are inevitably cases of unconventional promotion and reluctant acceptance. For example, Tang Yulin, who presented Jehol, is known to all as a notorious person who harmed the country! Since the loss of Jehol, calls for his arrest and punishment have spread throughout the country. However, rumors may not be entirely true, so the central government sent personnel to investigate thoroughly. It is likely that "no evidence was found." Perhaps "there are no great generals to resist Japan," so "a fleeing general is made a vanguard." Although the arrest warrant has not been rescinded, the position of army commander has been effectively bestowed.

From losing territory to investigation, from investigation to reappointing as army commander, this is a very clever approach. Although General Tang's fortune is somewhat unfavorable, his official star has not fallen. Losing the "chairmanship" (because there is no chair to preside over) and gaining the "army commander" is not entirely without consolation. Compared to the young Marshal Zhang who was blocked from going abroad, he is much more fortunate.

Moreover, the memorial contains the phrase "continue to resist Japan," which shows that the previous rumors of "fleeing upon seeing over a hundred enemies" were not true. The public is foolish, but the army commander is wise. Offending the tiger's might is a capital offense. However, future historians of the Republic of China can deduce from the phrase "continue to resist Japan" that he "once resisted Japan." Are those who resisted Japan not called national heroes? His name will undoubtedly be remembered for centuries. As for the monthly military expenditure of 100,000, it is not expensive. Although it is not enough to support an entire army of soldiers, it can sustain a family of eight (or sixteen or thirty-two) for a long time. Young Marshal Zhang does not seem to have such good fortune because he thought of going abroad to see the legs of foreign women and dance a few more times.

In short, Tang Yulin's journey from chairman to losing territory, from losing territory to being wanted, and from being wanted to being reappointed as army commander is now confirmed. It also shows the government's painstaking efforts to "concentrate national talent to resist foreign aggression." But the worrying thing is whether General Tang's strategy of "continue to resist Japan" will "continue" his past performance. Although we, the common people, are called "fools," we are quite concerned.

Feeling Inspired After Seeing Four Poems by Mr. Yong'an of Guiyang, Expressing My Thoughts Through Poetry 265

— Wang Junqing

Living beings are deluded, dreaming of wealth and power, you alone drift away from the emperor's side. Rather imitate the Western Mountain, eating bitter ferns, than bow to the East Sea, reviving withered mulberries. Sovereignty is seized, a weak king is made a pawn, the record of slavery is clear, the Manchu race is disgraced. Cherish the fragrance of late-blooming chrysanthemums, ashamed of Zheng Wu's extravagance.

Worrying about trivial gains and losses like a chicken pecking at insects, I am known as a useless old thing. I mocked politicians for their early betrayal of their times, dared to call revolutionaries treacherous schemers. Seeking help from Shunshui, which country is appropriate? I am ashamed to be like Gu Yanwu, responsible for this body. I laugh at myself for busying myself ten times in autumn, Chang'e has little connection with me.

The Simplest Method for Converting Between Yuan and Liang 266

— Ding Chong

Recently, several methods for converting between yuan and liang have been published in this newspaper. However, these methods are either circuitous and complicated or require memorizing complicated formulas. I believe everyone considers them inadequate. Now, I will explain the method I want to use and discuss it with everyone. If you think it is the "simplest method for converting between yuan and liang," please use it to facilitate bookkeeping.

According to the current reform of abolishing the tael and adopting the yuan, it is stipulated that 0.715 taels of silver are equivalent to 1 silver yuan, which means that each tael of silver is worth 1.3986 yuan. This is only 0.0014 yuan less than 1.4 yuan. In mathematical terms, this is a difference of one thousandth. If each tael of silver is multiplied by 1.4, subtracting one-thousandth from the product will give 1.3986 yuan. Following this analogy, regardless of how many taels of silver there are, using the above method, one multiplication and one subtraction, will immediately yield the desired result. Let's demonstrate with an example:

Question: There are 356 taels of silver. How many silver yuan is this equivalent to?

356 × 1.4 = 498.4 498.4 - 0.4984 = 497.9016 yuan

The abbreviated calculation is:

(356 × 1.4) - (356 × 0.0014) = 498.4 - 0.4984 = 497.9016 yuan

As demonstrated by the above example, this simple method provides an accurate conversion between yuan and liang. Moreover, only one number needs to be memorized: "1.4" and the subtracted "one-thousandth." Also, with the "one-thousandth," you only need to recognize the position. The size of the number will be the same as the digits in the product, making it very easy to calculate.

Responsibility 267

— Zhenbang

The sun shines on the west window of our classroom, and the row of seats next to the wall is bathed in the warm sunlight. The school's disciplinary officers have also taken their posts. I was absorbed in "In Darkness," because the content of this book was truly miserable. So, I took a breath of fresh air by the west window. Suddenly, a classmate wearing glasses, with a Chinese-style top and a Western-style bottom (truly a combination of East and West), and a national salvation aviation badge, a school badge, and a disciplinary officer badge all shining brightly in the white light on his long gown. What a presence! What a debonair!

However, he was holding a large piece of coal ash in his hand and throwing it into the alley. After a while, he turned back and picked up another piece, continuing to throw it into the alley. So, one piece, two pieces, three pieces, four pieces, ... and from the alley, one piece, two pieces, three pieces, four pieces, ... were returned.

A primary school student next to him cried. He -- the classmate -- the brave disciplinary officer seemed to be unaware of this sound and continued his game of throwing.

"Ding-dong! ... Ding-dong! ...!" The preparatory bell rang, and the disciplinary officer's service time was over. -- This is stipulated by the school authorities. When the preparatory bell rings, the disciplinary officers must rest! -- Strange! His work -- his game was also stopped by the ding-dong bell!

Ah! Is that what the responsibility of a disciplinary officer is supposed to be?!

Scars of a Spring Night's Dream 268

— Xian

To greedily admire the peach blossoms, I quickened my pace, leaving my companions behind. This was an unknown peach grove, which many people come to admire every season, but like the Peach Blossom Spring, not a few people mysteriously get lost here every year. I walked slowly, the sky was already darkening; my companions had not caught up, and fearing I would lose my way, I stopped to wait for them. Suddenly, a thin, middle-aged man walked towards me, asking sternly, "What are you doing?" I told him that I was watching the peach blossoms and had lost my companions. He changed his expression and said with a smile, "You are lost too, come and sit at my house." Without hesitation, I followed him to a small house. Inside were many people, all looking at me with surprise. The thin, middle-aged man told them the reason, and a child jumped up and said, "This person might be a spy, causing big trouble like last year." The middle-aged man said kindly, "Sir, let us search you." I didn't know what was going on, but after they searched me, the middle-aged man told me, "This place is very far from your China. We are called the Old Country, and we have a small emperor who controls everything. Fearing that the people will rebel, he often sends spies to investigate. Last year, someone like you, sir, came here and got lost, and later caused big trouble; so we are very cautious with you, sir. Please forgive us."

I forgot about my companions who were left behind; I forgot how I would return; and I became curious about the little emperor. That there was still such an autocratic country, I asked the middle-aged man what their political situation was like.

"Isn't everything still decided by the little emperor's will?" he said, "Whether it's domestic or foreign affairs, whatever the little emperor says is what goes."

"Won't the people revolt?"

"What?"

I knew he didn't understand what "revolt" meant, so I used his own words and asked, "Won't the people resist?"

"On the one hand, he uses secret agents to investigate, and on the other hand, he sets up a high jump machine in public places, allowing people with the ability to jump; the higher they jump, the higher the position they get. As a result, a group of idle people have practiced this skill; even scholars who have read many books can't compare. He has gathered this group of capable people to obey him, so no one dares to resist anymore."

"That's good!" I said, "If idle people become officials, they will wear good clothes, eat good food, obey the little emperor, and won't trample on society anymore."

"Sir, you are truly a foreigner! You only know one thing, but not the other. Those who know the law and break it are even worse than us ordinary people. They pretend to obey the little emperor, swindle his money, and then they collude to exploit us ordinary people. The little emperor trusts them, so who can we ordinary people complain to?" The middle-aged man's eyes filled with tears as he spoke, almost crying.

Suddenly, it seemed as if the door was surrounded, and a shout of "Catch the counter-revolutionaries, catch the counter-revolutionaries!" came from outside. The middle-aged man turned pale with fright.

"Bang!" A gunshot exploded in the air, I opened my eyes and found myself sleeping on the bed in my clothes, a novel in my hand fell to the floor, the clock pointed to eleven o'clock, the wind and rain were raging outside the window, and the unclosed glass window was banging.

Shop Clerk Correspondence

Only Seen the Small, But Not the Big 269

Editor Sir:

I am a young child who has lived a hard life since I was young. Since my father lost his job, the economic situation at home has been very difficult. When I was fourteen, I went to work as an apprentice in the Western restaurant of a certain steamer. The acting comprador was very kind, and seeing that I had no hope of success there, he was kind enough to introduce me to your company in this port as a trainee. This company is really too big, so it is divided into many parts; it must be my fate, the head of my department is too outrageous. Every day when he comes to the company, he only knows how to drink and smoke, and doesn't care about official business. Our trainees' work is equivalent to doing his personal chores; buying wine, buying food, we are constantly busy. One day he asked me to buy wine, but the weather was not good, and it started to rain heavily, so my clothes were completely soaked from top to bottom, and I couldn't find an inch of dry space. To my misfortune, the supervisor happened to see me. I immediately hid the wine bottle; unexpectedly, he saw that I was soaked and thought I was playing outside, so he reprimanded me severely. This delayed the time for a long time, so the head of my department was also very angry and kept scolding me. I had to swallow this anger and tears. Unexpectedly, the company seems to ignore this kind of department head who gets paid but doesn't do anything, but our small employees' mistakes are severely investigated: by the end of the month, I was fired! Alas! Sir, as I write this, I am almost crying without tears, please advise me. Respectfully, Shen Guoli.

Editor's Note: Being a slave is of course very hard, but if you are a slave to one party, there is always a way to deal with it. The most unfortunate thing is to be a slave to many parties; pleasing this party will inevitably offend that party, and pleasing that party will inevitably offend this party. When we are in this situation, we must know our dangerous position, seek survival in death, and at least get rid of one of the constraints. Even if things don't work out and we are harmed, we must understand that this is a difficulty that we will encounter sooner or later, and there is no room for regret. If Mr. Shen had told the company authorities about the head of the department's situation, he might have been praised. Even if you don't want to offend anyone, then when you are seen and scolded by the supervisor, you should have told the truth. Now you have always protected him, but he is afraid that he will not have any sympathy for your dismissal! Mr. Shen's situation is now a foregone conclusion and cannot be saved; we hope that you will know how to deal with yourself when you encounter this situation again in the future. At the same time, we also hope that those in power must focus on the big picture when evaluating the performance of their subordinates: even if a small employee occasionally plays for a moment, it will not cause a big impact; but if a department head drinks and smokes all day long, it must be rectified!

Near News of the Desert Literary Society: The inaugural issue of the Desert Literary Semimonthly, edited by the Desert Literary Society, was originally scheduled to be published on the 1st, but was delayed until the 16th of this month due to an error by the printing house. The content is rich and the price is low. It includes Zhao Ji's "The Road Ahead for Chinese Literature and Art", Wu Chen's "The Scarlet Lips in the Wind and Rain", "The Wild Geese in Spring", the long historical novel "The Heavenly Kingdom", and sketches of writers such as Qian Bixian and Gao Erji Hua Sui. Each issue is priced at two cents. The annual subscription, including postage, costs five jiao. Those who subscribe for the whole year before the end of April will also receive Dan Chun's "Spring Serenade of Love" as a souvenir. To promote the magazine, the first issue will be given away free of charge. Please attach postage when requesting by mail. The distribution is at No. 11, E, Old Schubert Road, Pike Road. The magazine is also sold in major newspapers in this port.

Novel

Fleeting Time in Dreams (Continued 29) 270

— Qin Shouou

If it were someone else, they would certainly not want to hold this empty title with great power falling by the wayside, but Wu Yi根本 (genben, fundamentally) did not hope to seize any power, so he felt very comfortable. Every day, he would hide in his office alone, drinking a little wine and returning home drunk. However, once he became the principal, a group of people paid attention to him. Before long, the nickname "Brandy Principal" became as well-known as "Christian General" and "Monk Dean" in Nanjing.

(13) The Lover's Son

Boxes of brandy, wrapped in silver paper and tied with straw all around, were transported from the foreign goods store. In a few days, they would all be empty and carried away by the junk collectors. Wu Yi's puppet-like leadership life passed by like a dream in such a simple environment.

I can't remember how many years have passed, but I know that the short hair on Wu Yi's head has changed from a small half white and a large half black to a large half white and a small half black. This year, the political stage in China has, as usual, seen another change of famous actors, which is not surprising at all; but this change of cast had a small impact on Wu Yi. It turned out that his old boss, the Minister of Education, had spent the past few years safely overcoming four or five difficult hurdles and maintaining his original position, but this time, unexpectedly, the President of the Executive Yuan sent him a directive to "immediately suspend his duties and await further appointment." So he had to roll out of office, and his departure also took away the two director-generals around Wu Yi. When they left, Wu Yi also hurriedly packed his things, preparing to leave, because he expected that when the new minister took office, he, the ancestral tablet-like university president, would have to give way to another talent. Who knew that this new minister was precisely a former student of his at the XX Political School, and still a tenderfoot official who had just taken office. Seeing the teacher-student relationship, he was embarrassed to ask him to leave. In addition to sending his younger brother to be the director of general affairs, he also returned half of the power over academic affairs to Wu Yi. This really made Wu Yi both happy and afraid as he held his wine glass.

Before, if someone asked him: "About how many students are there in your school?" Or: "Which students in your school are more active?" his answer would definitely be a shake of his head: because besides sitting in the principal's office drinking, he didn't care about anything else, and actually, it wasn't his turn to care. So he didn't even know how many professors and hundreds of students there were in his school. Since his proud student had returned half of his political power to him, he gradually got a clue, and at the same time, he also discovered that his eldest son, Wu Yuan, was a senior in the third year of the school, and also a very active backbone member of the student union.

Wu Yi was truly a pitiful person with many twists and turns in his fate. When he was a puppet, the school affairs of X University were very smooth, and there were never any unfortunate incidents. After he sat in the golden palace and personally attended court, serious problems followed. The first and most difficult was the students' patriotic movement.

Film Special

Skills That Struggle with Life 271

— Hua Ming

The first person in Hollywood to have adventurous stunts was Bob Rose. During the silent film era, he caused a sensation in countries around the world in "Avenging Arrow" and "Haunted Valley." At that time, he was an actor and was with Universal Pictures. After these two films came out, Bob performed in New York and almost lost his life due to carelessness. He was seriously injured and was forced to rest and recuperate in a mental institution for more than a year. After his recovery, stunt films in Hollywood declined. Although a few were made, they were all insignificant.

Although Bob Rose did not work in Hollywood after his recovery, he was only about thirty years old and still had ambitions. How could he give up and bury his skills? So he was eager to try. RKO Pictures was looking for talent in this area due to the lack of stunt films. As soon as they learned that Bob's health had recovered, they immediately sent someone to invite him. Bob agreed, and it was just what he wanted.

The first stunt film that RKO hired Bob Rose to perform in was called "Lucky Devils." In addition to Bob, the actors were all well-known experts in American martial arts. However, after the actors were determined, the director could not be found despite repeated efforts. Ordinary directors were not competent, and good directors had no experience in stunts. In the end, RKO sent Bob to take on the role himself. Bob did not decline and readily accepted. "Lucky Devils" does not have terrible makeup, nor does it use scientific equipment to create terrible shapes, but from beginning to end, there is not a single scene that does not make people's hair stand on end. Jumping out of a plane, jumping from this plane to that plane, jumping off the top of a speeding train, rolling down from the top of a high, steep cliff in the mountains, falling into a huge waterfall. If it were off by a fraction of an inch, it would hit a sharp mountain rock and could immediately turn into meat paste.

After "Lucky Devils" was completed, although it went through many dangerous situations, fortunately, all the actors were only injured and did not sacrifice their lives. Bob was also slightly injured during work, but he did not rest. Two actors almost drowned in the raging tide several feet high, which was the most dangerous moment of the entire work.

Film Review

Re-Review of "The Great Man" 272

— Li Qiong

It is very obvious that in order to meet the progressive needs of the general audience, Chinese films such as "Fire Burning" and "Great Swordsman" have lost their appeal. The Yueming Company, which has always strived for "Great Swordsman of the Guandong", has also had to change direction and engage in love stories.

Of course, we do not deny that love affairs can sometimes meet the needs of movies, and can even enrich the content of the film with love as the outer garment. However, the makers of "The Great Man" completely fail to understand these important points, and only attempt to somersault in the mire of multi-faceted love affairs. Of course, there will be no new tricks discovered.

The story itself is very nonsensical, so the progress on the screen is completely far-fetched. Although some of it depicts the fierceness of the warlord, it only describes some extremely unimportant and unreasonable events in which he helps his son grab a woman out of his doting love for his son, and it fails to grasp a greater center and promote the anti-warlord theme. Even in terms of details, such as Fan Tong calling himself his elder brother, 文柏's (Wen Bo's) "scheming" to earn money, and escaping in disguise, are all very ridiculous.

In terms of performance, of course, a perfect film cannot be performed based on a base story. The director's use of the camera is too unskilled in changing angles. He does not have a proper understanding of the roles in the play, so that the people in the play become nondescript in the direction of the performance. Most of the actors are too civilized and theatrical, especially Wang Dongxia, which makes people embarrassed. Many over-the-top performances inevitably make people cringe. Wu Lizhu's belly is too big, and she should have rested. Since this is the case, of course she cannot be lively. Both exterior and interior scenes are not good. The lighting is blurry, and there are too many and childish subtitles.

Overall, one cannot help but call it a "failure." However, compared to "Great Swordsman of the Guandong" and the like, it is still a step forward.

Audience Opinion

Further Discussion of "Storm Over Asia" 273

— Yao Yinzhong

Hope it can be shown everywhere in the mainland

The movies we usually watch are nothing more than "glamour," "sensuality," "romance," "mystery," etc. At best, these kinds of movies only show the breasts and jade legs of women, and the suits and top hats of gentlemen; they only show strong wine and intoxicating songs and dances! We can say that we have seen enough of this kind of movie, why not have movies that are the opposite to change our taste, such as "A New Life", "Reunion", which were shown in Shanghai in the past, and "Storm Over Asia", which is currently being shown? These Soviet Russian films can provide us with this kind of demand.

Really, Soviet Russian films are absolutely different from what we usually watch. Not only are the stories performed different, but the performance techniques are also different. They can not only change our taste, but also give us new and great inspirations!

"Storm Over Asia" is set in Mongolia, China, and vividly depicts how weak nations are subjected to the aggression and oppression of powerful capitalist imperialism, and how weak nations rise up to resist and defeat capitalist imperialism. This is indeed a rare and valuable good film. I hope that this film can continue to be shown everywhere in our country. At a time when the national crisis is serious, strong enemies are invading, and even more brutal, it can at least awaken the dreams of the general public and inspire the spirit of the general public.

Finally, I would also like to add a sentence: Foreigners have always liked to portray Chinese people in extremely ugly ways, making it impossible for people to swallow their meals, such as dragging long braids, smoking opium, and binding small feet. This film is the exact opposite everywhere. From this, we can also understand who is our friend in the world and who is our enemy.

Also, the original name of this film and the previous name, National Soul, are not very appropriate to my liking. It would be better to change it to "Asian National Soul." I wonder what the wise readers think? (Answer requested)

A General Review of "Storm Over Asia": Who Doesn't Feel Their Blood Boiling After Watching It? 274

The whole film does not have any flaws, but for the ending we want to ask: "Is the victory built on the wind really a victory?" The film probably had to end at this point. It was impossible to continue, and it would be depressing to say that the patriotic group was defeated by the White Army, so they had to borrow the power of the wind and sand. The director's means are extremely clever. The few scenes of duels are very tense, especially the scene where two people fight on a dangerous cliff and fall down, which is even more powerful. The few contrasting scenes also give us strong hints. The process of Temujin's execution by shooting is done slowly, but it is not loose. Step by step, it holds the audience's emotions and makes everyone unwilling to see Temujin die. A puppet transformed into a warrior, very naturally without idealistic elements. The stimulation of the Silver Fox is not enough. Killing a Mongolian in front of him is too stimulating for him, and then a crazy resistance breaks out. When Temujin rushes out, the audience's enthusiasm for resisting is stirred up by the mixed use of inverted and intricate subtitles and frantic waving.

I'm afraid there are very few people who don't feel their blood boiling after watching it? At a time when diplomatic relations between China and Japan have not been severed, the four northeastern provinces have been ceded, the volunteer army outside the Guan has been repeatedly oppressed, and the puppet is sitting firmly in Changchun, what kind of feelings and hints do our viewers get from this film that seems to be shot for us?

A Bunch of News from Various Companies 276

Tianyi News: Tianyi Film Company's new film "Vitality" has been working very hard under the supervision of Shao Zuiweng recently. The other day, forty temporary female actors were used for a scene at the factory gate. A certain introduction agency felt it was difficult to meet Tianyi's needs, because almost all the temporary female actors in Shanghai were accustomed to fashion, and it was really not easy to find many female actors in short clothes and worker appearances. Later, Tianyi shot an interior scene of the factory, requiring sixty female actors of that type. This time, the introduction agency was tired from running around to find them. As a result of searching from morning to night, a total of forty-eight people were found. In the end, they had to resort to kidnapping people to make up the numbers, and only then did they break through the difficult situation, but the scene of this group of short-clothed workers working in the factory was indeed great and realistic.

Jinan News: Jinan Company's "Winning Glory for the Country" has been in production for four months since it started filming last winter, but the economic situation has been bad, so it cannot be finished in one go. The other day, they shot the outdoor scene of the Volunteer Army departing in Longhua. It is said to be the last scene. The entire play was also filmed yesterday, and the release date should not be far away.

Mingxing News: A former employee and artist of Tianyi, Hu Zhuoyun, resigned from Tianyi and transferred to Mingxing. He has been promoted from artist to set designer. It is a pity that he has the temperament of an artist, so Zhang Shichuan is very dissatisfied with him. It is said that Hu Zhuoyun has left Mingxing again. His colleagues who entered Mingxing with Tianyi are very sorry for him.

— Zhou Jingzhi

It is said that Harry Banishter, an old star, is now over ninety years old. He still imitates romance, and he and his wife, Ann Harding, are divorcing in preparation to marry another Miss Nancy Lyon. It is said that she is only twenty years old and is a social butterfly. However, Harry Banishter said: "There is no such thing, there is no such thing, can ninety and twenty be in proportion?"

The Oldest Stars in the Film Industry 278

— Luo Xiu

There are really many old stars in the film industry, and the oldest one is the British old man Fred Kerr, who is already seventy-four years old this year. At the age of seventy, he was still able to perform on the screen, playing an old man. The second is C. Aubrey Smith. In the past few months, he has performed in seven films at the same time, although he is now seventy years old.

As for the world-famous Marie Dressler, she is already sixty-four years old this year, and she is still dominating the screen. The male star who can match her is George Arliss, who is also sixty-four years old this year, and his position in the film industry is almost equal.

Movie Novel Tarakanova (4) 279

— Mei Hua

General Grelg and Orlov's warships were anchored near Princess Raknarova's palace, like white geese floating on the water, adding a touch of elegance to the palace. Orlov, mingling with the cheering crowds, encountered Princess Tarakanova! Her alluring eyes reminded him of the Gypsy girl he had met during the Turkish war! At this moment, amidst the cheers and jumps of the crowd, singing Gypsy love songs, she disappeared in a flash, just like on the battlefield.

Orlov, arriving happily and leaving dejectedly, felt as if he had lost his soul. He thought to himself: "How did I meet her again? Isn't she the Gypsy girl I met at the front line that day? Heavens!" He finally exhausted all means to meet this beautiful princess. He poured all his spirit into her eyes. He recognized her, no, she recognized him too! From that moment on, Orlov visited the beautiful Princess Tarakanova every day, their hearts beating as one.

However, General Grelg, who had come with him, did not understand Orlov's feelings and kept urging him to lure Princess Raknarova back to Russia according to the pre-arranged plan! Torn between "love" and "loyalty to duty," Orlov hesitated for a long time. He dared not disobey Catherine, and finally invited Princess Raknarova to his warship. Princess Tarakanova accepted his request, adorned with pearls and emeralds, looking like a celestial being. She stepped onto the warship, laid out like a net of heaven and earth by General Grelg and Orlov. Cannons boomed, the national flag fluttered on the mast, and music drifted in the wind. Princess Raknarova dreamed of returning to Moscow and holding a grand coronation ceremony amidst the cheers of the crowd, with her lover Orlov following her closely!

However, such joyous moments are only a fleeting instant in life! Princess Raknarova only enjoyed this little bit. When the warship sailed into Russian territory, all the hideous and ugly faces broke through the beautiful façade. The lover who had always been considered gentle and kind now transformed into a sinister and treacherous poisonous creature.

Princess Tarakanova was captured. Although captured, she could not abandon her love for Orlov; indeed, Orlov was lovable. His handsome appearance and majestic figure were enough to make Tarakanova infatuated and unforgettable. However, Orlov's heart was also shattered like flower petals. Under Catherine's tyrannical power, he dared not resist her demands, and finally brought his lover, Princess Tarakanova, to meet her.
